
-----title
祁门 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0fbc97941b714cd4aa4eda1b130fb8cf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0fbc97941b714cd4aa4eda1b130fb8cf");'><span id='0fbc97941b714cd4aa4eda1b130fb8cf_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年11月30日</a>　方岳生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1205')">1199-1205年</a>　不详。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1206&endYear=1206')">1206年</a>　祖父卒，方岳作《祭诗》<div id='poem_64980' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64980' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/64980?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_64980")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_64980_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_64980'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_64980'>我生胡不辰，八龄失吾祖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_64980'>今垂四十年，眉目略可睹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64980'>当时深根培，所望大门户。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_64980'>岳也忝一科，遗馀曾不补。<div id='poem_sentence_3_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_64980'>而乃轻涛江，飞檄淮南府。<div id='poem_sentence_4_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_64980'>父兄肯相随，薄饭共贫苦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_64980'>宁知事大谬，俱作一抔土。<div id='poem_sentence_6_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_64980'>去年汶素跸，永痛松柏古。<div id='poem_sentence_7_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_64980'>禄釜亦已矣，尚安事圭组。<div id='poem_sentence_8_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_64980'>今年误一出，竟犯时辈怒。<div id='poem_sentence_9_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_64980'>去国不及炊，触热到环堵。<div id='poem_sentence_10_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_64980'>无何七月望，新露洒秋宇。<div id='poem_sentence_11_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_64980'>近郊有兰若，梵呗薄云雨。<div id='poem_sentence_12_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_64980'>彼氓一念存，提携颇旁午。<div id='poem_sentence_13_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_64980'>因果夫何如，亦各言恃怙。<div id='poem_sentence_14_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_64980'>伊予祖父兄，超然定何许。<div id='poem_sentence_15_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_64980'>然皆其忌月，悲岂不氓愈。<div id='poem_sentence_16_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_64980'>斋盂馔伊蒲，从众共伛偻。<div id='poem_sentence_17_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_64980'>盖以妄塞悲，有泪泚清酤<span class='inlineComment2'>（同上书卷一三）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_18_64980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_64980'></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_64980_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1207&endYear=1207')">1207年</a>　学于里东皋，识冯椅，是为岳启蒙师。乡人傩墨义，操笔立就，为之惊。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1208&endYear=1213')">1208-1213年</a>　不详。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1214&endYear=1214')">1214年</a>　方岳入郡庠，严陵叶子仪点请诸生复诵《通鉴》，唯方岳与方瑑能抗之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1215&endYear=1222')">1215-1222年</a>　不详。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1223&endYear=1223')">1223年</a>　方岳识袁甫始此。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1224&endYear=1224')">1224年</a>　宁宗崩，史弥远矫诏贵诚嗣位。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1226&endYear=1226')">1226年</a>　方岳秋闱落第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1227&endYear=1227')">1227年</a>　原籍歙城宝谟阁少卿汪中立来知徽州。方岳集中致诗八首，足见交深。卷二二《呈知郡汪少卿》写于是年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1228&endYear=1228')">1228年</a>　夏，为汪卿撰《秀锦楼赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（方岳青壮年时期，理学只生。方岳于朱（朱熹）门弟子婺源滕璘、滕珙、李季子、祁门谢琎和同辈学者滕和叔、程若庸、陈庆勉等，或师之，或友之，以是而学有渊源。）</span><div id='poem_1311587' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311587' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311587?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秀锦楼赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1228年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311587")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311587_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311587'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311587'>直宝谟阁汪侯守歙之明年，政恬事熙，民以嘉豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311587_comment'></div>间从宾客僚吏登城西北隅，挹其山川而乐之，喟然曰：吾先世郡人也，今吾适守于是，其得窃自比于昼锦之荣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311587_comment'></div>乃作秀锦之楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311587_comment'></div>楼成，大会宾客落之，而使其民方岳赋之，其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1311587'>俯春城之杳渺兮，溯碧溪之绀寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311587_comment'></div>搴<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1311587", 1311587, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>朝岚</span>与夕霏兮，秀色蔚其可餐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311587_comment'></div>挹浮丘而欲仙兮，抚玉蜍以盘桓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311587_comment'></div>曰山川其信美兮，吾曾祖之所家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311587_comment'></div>几何时其此去兮，窃空老于汀花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311587_comment'></div>鹤千载而来归兮，览城郭而长嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311587_comment'></div>皇畀予以左竹兮，岂锦衣之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1311587", 1311587, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>昼行</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311587_comment'></div>森戟卫之靓深兮，燕香阒其欲凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311587_comment'></div>眷童牙其予姓兮，耋老予之父兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311587_comment'></div>羌昵昵以儿语兮，肯自诧于新硎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311587_comment'></div>幸里党之我与兮，散佩犊于春耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311587_comment'></div>嘻无事其可了兮，寄吾笔于鸥盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311587_comment'></div>伟飞楼之耸翠兮，纳风烟于檐楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311587_comment'></div>洗古彝之娟碧兮，与畅叙其幽情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311587_comment'></div>激沙弹与豪吹兮，落孤啸于青冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311587_comment'></div>冈峦忽其翔舞兮，纷不暇于逢迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1311587_comment'></div>紫阳缭以西转兮，倚谪仙而自矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1311587_comment'></div>北黄山其六六兮，轩后轶而上征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1311587_comment'></div>岿问政之东峙兮，逗春雾于花屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1311587_comment'></div>飘吾袂以轻举兮，讯许聂乎深云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1311587_comment'></div>纫崇兰以为佩兮，缀明月而成缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1311587_comment'></div>受山气之朝爽兮，截鹭波之晚清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1311587_comment'></div>夕阳澹其未收兮，指素娥以将升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1311587_comment'></div>弄林影以扶醉兮，酹吾樽于江山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1311587_comment'></div>曰尧民其熙皞兮，吾何心于铸顽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1311587_comment'></div>鹿扰之则骇逝兮，鱼自乐于深潜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1311587_comment'></div>审左餐而右粥兮，桁杨卧而昼閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1311587_comment'></div>来牟蓊以相依兮，桑麻沃其蓁蓁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1311587_comment'></div>吾与客而乐此兮，觊枌社之皆春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1311587_comment'></div>公在楼而燕喜兮，民歌裤而遨嬉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1311587_comment'></div>孰有笔其如椽兮，梯青壁而劖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1311587_comment'></div>酾练江以为寿兮，取玉兔以为卮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1311587_comment'></div>起祝公其少留兮，聊暇日以委蛇。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1311587_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1229&endYear=1229')">1229年</a>　歙人程元凤、休宁人程若颜、黟人汪昱均登黄朴榜进士（《徽州府志》），方岳再次落第。其《酹江月·和君用》即针对史弥远弄权，致使自己屡败场屋而发。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1229&endYear=1229')">1229年2月</a>　范钟知徽州，绍定四年四月诏除刑部郎中（《徽州府志》）。方岳与之相识始于范守徽期间。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='689a34b616064803989c3aa46cec7489_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("689a34b616064803989c3aa46cec7489");'><span id='689a34b616064803989c3aa46cec7489_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1240')">1239-1240年</a>，42-43岁</div><div id='689a34b616064803989c3aa46cec7489' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>　方岳于是年秋天返回故里，侍父病。寻父卒，丁忧。作品：《陶倅母夫人挽诗》<div id='poem_64964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/64964?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陶倅母夫人挽诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_64964")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_64964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_64964'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_64964'>戴君手持黄卿辞，邀我为作陶母诗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_64964'>妇言妇德不出梱，纵有令则何繇知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64964'>昆山生玉草木润，欲识其母观其儿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_64964'>一经科目摘髭易，五丈夫子皆瑰奇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_64964'>黄卿与世少谐可，老笔为写青琉璃。<div id='poem_sentence_4_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_64964'>嘅予一读恍如洗，酸风凄断漳淮湄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_64964'>往年将父问里舍，病痱中道惊相持。<div id='poem_sentence_6_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_64964'>秋山黯惨过县尹，取急欲谒谁何医。<div id='poem_sentence_7_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_64964'>天方罪予不孝子，行未半驿翁阽危。<div id='poem_sentence_8_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_64964'>云崩日落竟千古，永始此路行无期。<div id='poem_sentence_9_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_64964'>尔时县尹有母遗，鲐背儿齿当期颐。<div id='poem_sentence_10_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_64964'>潘舆佳日访桃李，一舍而迎聊遨嬉。<div id='poem_sentence_11_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_64964'>人间仅仅几寒暑，亦已奔月归何时。<div id='poem_sentence_12_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_64964'>暮云春树渺千里，同一哀痛难平治。<div id='poem_sentence_13_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_64964'>此诗莫遣挽郎读，天荒地老松风悲。<div id='poem_sentence_14_64964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_64964'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_64964_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>　赵范叙复官职，与宫观，方岳为之作《赵龙学落宫观谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（是年，吴文英四十岁。正月与吴潜观梅沧浪亭，作《金缕歌》，潜有贺章。）</span><div id='poem_1311618' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311618' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311618?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赵龙学落宫观谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311618")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311618_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311618'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311618'>囊封自劾，分投荒裔之居；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311618_comment'></div>纶旨载颁，仅削真庭之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311618_comment'></div>感宽恩之天大，陨孤涕以雨如<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311618_comment'></div>臣本乏修能，误叨重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311618_comment'></div>有死耳不可屈，每思马革而裹之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311618_comment'></div>今老矣无能为，岂知鼯技之穷已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311618_comment'></div>粤临岘首，遄警旄头，悲环城皆虎视之乡，列郡尽鸿哀之宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311618_comment'></div>祸一至于此极，身百战以何裨！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311618_comment'></div>赖国之威，彼师其遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311618_comment'></div>而臣材不足以御众，智不足以察奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311618_comment'></div>羝羊触藩，尚骇塞垣之未靖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311618_comment'></div>虎兕出柙，讵图家贼之难防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311618_comment'></div>变忽起于萧墙，势竟隳于屏翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311618_comment'></div>擢发以数，噬脐莫追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311618_comment'></div>思昔先臣，久兹分梱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311618_comment'></div>析薪罔克负荷，孰云泉壤之无知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311618_comment'></div>稽田既勤敷菑，窃叹金汤之安在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311618_comment'></div>谓且赐属镂而肆市，不然御魑魅于九区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311618_comment'></div>敢意圣朝，屈从轻典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1311618_comment'></div>此盖恭遇皇帝仁深在宥，德洽好生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1311618_comment'></div>意若曰美及子孙，盍稽八议；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1311618_comment'></div>幸无以累遗君父，姑缓五刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1311618_comment'></div>迄回物论以并包，用贷微躯于显戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1311618_comment'></div>臣敢不省厥愆于羁旅，终其老于累囚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1311618_comment'></div>念死有馀辜，莫寝遐方之梗化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1311618_comment'></div>傥生无以报，当为厉鬼以灭雠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1311618_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年3月</a>　吴潜为敷文歌学士，沿海制置使兼知庆元府，方岳作《贺吴阁学》<div id='poem_1311759' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311759' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311759?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺吴阁学启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311759")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311759_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311759'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311759'>伏睹邸函，显跻册府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311759_comment'></div>二三谟典，于皇继序之传；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311759_comment'></div>百万甲兵，增重提纲之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311759_comment'></div>遹通班于曳履，殆举国以弹冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311759_comment'></div>抑人有言，方时多事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311759_comment'></div>共慨四郊之多垒，遗君父忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311759_comment'></div>谁为万里之长城，卫行在所？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311759_comment'></div>表里正资于外御，本根尤急于内宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311759_comment'></div>惟浙东西，在帝左右，既久狃安于畿甸，曾微穿朽之干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311759_comment'></div>顾今当艰难之时，安可习承平之故！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311759_comment'></div>乃升延阁，诞诘戎兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311759_comment'></div>虽以文章鸣国家，固吾君之亲擢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311759_comment'></div>然而忠信为甲胄，非真儒而孰归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311759_comment'></div>行矣登庸，式宏经济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311759_comment'></div>某隔兹衣带之水，莫旅簪缨之尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311759_comment'></div>丕显哉文王谟，喜峻直西清之邃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311759_comment'></div>归来乎太公望，岂久为北固之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311759_comment'></div>侧耳思言，驰心丈席。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1311759_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年3月</a>　别之杰权兵部尚书，依旧沿江制置安抚使兼都督行府参赞军事，方岳作《与别制置》<div id='poem_1312013' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312013' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312013?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与别制置劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312013")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312013_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312013'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312013'>某属耳贽书于签府，意谓敌为不道，荐食上国，夷我关陇，残我汉沔，敢于凭陵无厌者，正以诸公袖手于绿野之闲，冥心于墨缞之惨，而上流是用急也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312013_comment'></div>使星西行，芒寒色正，彼虽倨傲自恣，然仗我国威，亦既詟胆而夺之气矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312013_comment'></div>梁襄王问孟轲氏曰：「天下恶乎定」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312013_comment'></div>曰：「定于一」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312013_comment'></div>「孰能一之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312013_comment'></div>曰：「不嗜杀人者能一之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312013_comment'></div>伊彼敌人，惟残惟忍，负戎马足，所过无噍类焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312013_comment'></div>彼苍者天，宁不蹙额于此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312013_comment'></div>祸盈之极，不能终日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312013_comment'></div>伏惟钺下一世声名，草木震叠，乃敌王忾，歼此鞠凶，使边境永清，复见平世，则旂常鼎鼐有不胜载者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312013_comment'></div>惟为国家勉图之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1312013_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年5月</a>　吴潜为兵部尚书，浙西制置使，再知镇江府，方岳作《贺吴尚书》，另有《木兰花慢·吴尚书宴涟沧观》作品：《贺吴尚书》、《木兰花慢·吴尚书宴涟沧观》<div id='poem_65085' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_65085' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/65085?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新郎<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>寄两吴尚书</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_65085'>雁向愁边落。<div id='poem_sentence_0_65085_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_65085'>渺汀洲、孤云细雨，暮天寒角。<div id='poem_sentence_1_65085_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_65085'>有美人兮山翠外，谁共霜桥月壑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_65085_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_65085'>想朋友、春猿秋鹤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_65085_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_65085'>竹屋一灯棋未了，问人间、局面如何著。<div id='poem_sentence_4_65085_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_65085'>风雨夜，更商略。<div id='poem_sentence_5_65085_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_65085'>六州铁铸从头错。<div id='poem_sentence_6_65085_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_65085'>笑归来、冰鲈堪鲙，雪螯堪嚼。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_65045' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/65045?labeling=true' target='_blank'>木兰花慢 吴尚书宴客涟沧观，即席用韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_65045")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_65045_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_65045'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_65045'>慨晴江渺渺，乘风下、倚沧浪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_65045_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_65045'>问许大乾坤，金焦两点，曾几兴亡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_65045_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_65045_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年8月</a>　以游似参知政事，方岳作《回游参政》<span class='inlineComment2'>（游似，字景仁，四川利州人，嘉定十四年进士，历任吏部、吏部尚书。嘉佑五年任右相兼枢密使。）</span><div id='poem_1312044' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312044' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312044?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回游参政劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1312044'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312044'>某自未脱民伍，已知世有程伯淳，盖陈和仲司成时时为道一世名卿大夫，公相其首也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312044_comment'></div>某也贱，执御无繇，于今十七八年，司成之言故在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312044_comment'></div>适有天幸，起从田间，会正人登庸，善类幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312044_comment'></div>然曳裾门下者于再于四，未得一望末光，退然惧且惭，莫知所以。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312044_comment'></div>敢图夹袋收录，俾上名氏，某极知其僭，而盛心其敢不承？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312044_comment'></div>惟钧慈贳之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1312044_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年</a>　居家丁父忧，方岳作《哨遍·问月》<div id='poem_65088' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_65088' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/65088?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哨遍<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>问月</a><span class='authorDate'>（1240年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_65088")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_65088_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_65088'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_65088'>月亦老乎，劝尔一杯，听说平生事。<div id='poem_sentence_0_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_65088'>吾问汝，开辟自何时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_65088'>有乾坤更应有尔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_65088'>年几许。<div id='poem_sentence_3_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_65088'>鸿荒邈哉遐已。<div id='poem_sentence_4_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_65088'>吾今断自唐虞起。<div id='poem_sentence_5_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_65088'>繄帝曰放勋，甲辰践祚，数至今、宋嘉熙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_65088'>凡三千五百二十年馀。<div id='poem_sentence_7_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_65088'>嗟雨僽风僝几盈亏。<div id='poem_sentence_8_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_65088'>老兔奔驰，痴蟆吞吐，定应衰矣。<div id='poem_sentence_9_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_65088'>噫。<div id='poem_sentence_10_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_65088'>月岂无悲。<div id='poem_sentence_11_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_65088'>吾观人寿几期颐。<div id='poem_sentence_12_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_65088'>炯炯双眸子，明清无过婴儿。<div id='poem_sentence_13_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_65088'>但才到中年，昏然欲眊，那堪老矣知何似。<div id='poem_sentence_14_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_65088'>试以此推之。<div id='poem_sentence_15_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_65088'>吾言有理，不能不自疑耳。<div id='poem_sentence_16_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_65088'>恐古时月与今时异。<div id='poem_sentence_17_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_65088'>阿谁曾自前古，看到隋唐世。<div id='poem_sentence_20_65088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1242&endYear=1242')">1242年</a>　，此后，壬（本年）、癸、甲、乙四年均在家乡闲居。方岳有《哨遍·用韻作月对和程申父国録》<div id='poem_65089' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_65089' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/65089?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哨遍<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>用韵作月对和程申父国录</a><span class='authorDate'>（1242年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_65089")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_65089_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_65089'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_65089'>月曰不然，君亦怎知，天上从前事。<div id='poem_sentence_0_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_65089'>吾语汝，月岂有弦时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_65089'>奈人间井观乃尔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_65089'>休浪许。<div id='poem_sentence_3_65089_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_65089'>妄相传、月溯日光馀。<div id='poem_sentence_7_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_65089'>嗟万古谁知了无亏。<div id='poem_sentence_8_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_65089'>玉斧修成，银蟾奔去，此言荒矣。<div id='poem_sentence_9_65089_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_65089'>噫。<div id='poem_sentence_10_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_65089'>世已堪悲。<div id='poem_sentence_11_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_65089'>听君歌复解人颐。<div id='poem_sentence_12_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_65089'>桂魄何曾死，寒光不减些儿。<div id='poem_sentence_13_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_65089'>但与日相望，对如两镜，山河大地无疑似。<div id='poem_sentence_14_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_65089'>待既望观之。<div id='poem_sentence_15_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_65089'>冰轮渐侧，转斜才一钩耳。<div id='poem_sentence_16_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_65089'>论本来不与中秋异。<div id='poem_sentence_17_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_65089'>恐天问灵均未知此。<div id='poem_sentence_18_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_65089'>又底用、咸池重洗。<div id='poem_sentence_19_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_65089'>乾坤一点英气。<div id='poem_sentence_20_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_65089'>宁老人间世。<div id='poem_sentence_21_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_65089'>飞上天来，摩挲月去，才信有晴无雨。<div id='poem_sentence_22_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_65089'>人生圆缺几何其。<div id='poem_sentence_23_65089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_65089'>且徘徊、与君同醉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_65089_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1243&endYear=1243')">1243年</a>　在家闲居。作品：《行香子·癸卯生日》<div id='poem_65066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_65066' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/65066?labeling=true' target='_blank'>行香子 癸卯生日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1243年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_65066")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_65066_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_65066'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_65066'>说与樵青。<div id='poem_sentence_0_65066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_65066'>紧闭柴门。<div id='poem_sentence_1_65066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_65066'>道先生检校东屯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_65066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_65066'>阿戎安在，未扫愁痕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_65066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_65066'>且免歌词，休载妓，莫携樽。<div id='poem_sentence_4_65066_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_65066'>梅自生春。<div id='poem_sentence_5_65066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_65066'>雪立前村。<div id='poem_sentence_6_65066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_65066'>道此杯、酒也须温。<div id='poem_sentence_7_65066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_65066'>无穷身外，付与乾坤。<div id='poem_sentence_8_65066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_65066'>谁共耕山，闲钓水、饱窥园。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_65066_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1243&endYear=1243')">1243年6月</a>　在家闲居，为同邑壬方元美作《莱山堂记》<div id='poem_1312336' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312336' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312336?labeling=true' target='_blank'>方氏莱山堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1243年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312336")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312336_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312336'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312336'>吾宗元美入蜀之年，款吾扉而西也，为之烹伏雌相劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312336_comment'></div>意其单车为万里别，不能无惘惘然者，顾作而言曰：「某解边县印绶属耳，既筑屋于溪居之北山，取《诗》所谓『北山有莱』者而谥之『莱山堂』，子为我言其意」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312336_comment'></div>予曰：「元美之为是也，将为隐乎，则方溯瞿唐、滟滪而上，访诸葛公平沙之石蕝而考求曹、刘诸人褒斜出入之涂，此其意未休也，子何有于莱？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312336_comment'></div>将为仕乎，则山人去而蕙帐空矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312336_comment'></div>意其碧丛翠颖，遗风罢月，而子搂之以为名莱，且有辞于子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312336_comment'></div>虽然，古之人不必隐时而隐，不必仕时而仕，莘野一犁之雨，磻溪一丝之风，盖将终焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312336_comment'></div>及丹书陈，溪惟空碧耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312336_comment'></div>《伊训》作，野惟寒青耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312336_comment'></div>是以君子有感于时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312336_comment'></div>《诗》固曰『南山有台，北山有莱，乐只君子，邦家之基』，此成王、周公极治之时乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312336_comment'></div>故其山中之人方且出而观凫鹥假乐之光以媚于天子，则其所谓台、莱者，夫固诗人所以兴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312336_comment'></div>勉旃行矣，子毋谓古远」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312336_comment'></div>乃为《反招隐》以寄声北山之莱曰：莱萋萋兮山之幽，翩王孙兮驾言西州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312336_comment'></div>松桂寒兮蛟龙樛，嘻山中兮不可以久留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312336_comment'></div>莱艾兮山之扉，渺王孙兮孤鹤与飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312336_comment'></div>芙蓉裳兮芰荷衣，微山中兮云谁之思！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312336_comment'></div>是岁淳祐三年夏六月乙丑，里人方岳记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1312336_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1243&endYear=1243')">1243年11月</a>　在家闲居。作《淮东转运使干办公事吴公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1312371' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312371' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312371?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉议郎淮东转运司干办公事吴公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳祐三年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312371")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312371_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312371'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312371'>予顷佐淮东军，休宁吴伯玉干饟餫，间以事白府，辄过予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312371_comment'></div>予辄为具鸡黍，酒行，辄撑拒曰：「平生毋酒，长毋多酌我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312371_comment'></div>然觉其意酣如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312371_comment'></div>最后望其面深墨，与之揖，三引其气而语廑属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312371_comment'></div>既坐，阁阁然喘不休，径起索舆去，留之饭不可，无几日公亡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312371_comment'></div>于是绍祖适归里，旁无强近之亲，予白府移书漕台，属西干主后事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312371_comment'></div>两司赙特厚，歛以无憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312371_comment'></div>是岁端平三年也，年六十有六矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312371_comment'></div>公讳天球，伯玉字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312371_comment'></div>曾大父某，大父某，父某，诸父连取科目，伯氏天骥为尚书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312371_comment'></div>公登嘉定七年进士第，官自修职郎至奉议郎，历庐州庐江尉、提点坑冶司检踏官、淮东转运司干办公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312371_comment'></div>公于是将遂亨矣，事有大谬不然，可为流涕痛哭者，盖不为公惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312371_comment'></div>国家失汴，至是百有馀年，未有窥左足向夷门一步者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312371_comment'></div>朝议以三梱兵复三京，凡淮东、泗、宿、宋、永、南北军之在行者，赵公葵实将之，遂以公为随军钱粮受给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312371_comment'></div>中原沦胥久，河失故道，运漕绝五河口，溯大小清河，略葛驿以达于京师，绵千数百里无人烟，率虎豹所嗥、鱼龙所家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312371_comment'></div>军无乏兴，遂入汴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312371_comment'></div>赵公于是盛服行宫阙，省宗庙，吊遗黎故老，以布宣明天子威德，亦一时之盛已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312371_comment'></div>方是时，将下制书，定功令，而潼关以败闻，赵公遂班师，公事格矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312371_comment'></div>不然，岂直一升朝官哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312371_comment'></div>公以某年月日生，某年月日殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312371_comment'></div>二子前卒，其承重者孤孙绍祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312371_comment'></div>以淳祐三年十二月甲子，葬县之睦亲里富潭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312371_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1312371'>能否人也，穷达天也，成败时也，离合机也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1312371_comment'></div>允乘尔时，而孰揠之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1312371_comment'></div>允投尔机，而孰蹳之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1312371_comment'></div>翼翼神京，既挈以伦，劳而不勋，其天其人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1312371_comment'></div>我穷曷嗟，黍离之复，复哉复哉，有瞑其目。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1312371_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年</a>　在家闲居，九月，史崇之以父病，谒告，许之。十二月，诏许崇之终丧，方岳作《与徐常卿》（元杰自将作监兼右司郎官，拜太常少卿）<div id='poem_1311958' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311958' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311958?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与徐常卿书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1244年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311958")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311958_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311958'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311958'>某辱出榜下，十有三年，忧患之故多于平时，废放之日长于仕宦，潜深伏隩，几与世相忘矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311958_comment'></div>以故不惟莫之见，而亦莫之书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311958_comment'></div>异时伦魁有不十年册拜者，虽太常不是卿，未足为执事者贺，平生之志不在温饱，亦未足为执事者惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311958_comment'></div>独有一事，不得不为时惜而为吾道贺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311958_comment'></div>芸夫荛子，乃有能传写常卿奏篇至林下者，读之三返不能已，其纡馀而有味，优柔而得体，真所谓朝阳之鸣凤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311958_comment'></div>皋夔以来远矣，试数我朝之一二公，若司马，若文、富，盖一代之名相，百世之名士，举动小差，初非有得罪于名教，失身于憸险者，而已若是，况所谓王荆公者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311958_comment'></div>士习陵夷，廉耻道丧，喑喑嘿嘿，惟利之趣，未有如今日之甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311958_comment'></div>遂使天下之公论，溢出于草茅者之口，撞搪叫号，不顾事体，则士大夫激之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311958_comment'></div>常卿不出此奏，则是举朝皆仗马也，皆辕驹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311958_comment'></div>万钟而下，一命而上，垂绅正笏而立于朝者，不知其几何人，而能为上一言者仅仅一徐常卿，是可不为时惜而为吾道贺哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311958_comment'></div>冬候暖然如春，愿毋爽调护，以栋干吾道，以圭玉斯文。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1311958_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年</a>　在家闲居，为本邑珠溪寺僧才老作《只恁么轩记》<div id='poem_1312337' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312337' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312337?labeling=true' target='_blank'>只恁么轩记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1244年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312337")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312337_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312337'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312337'>秋崖老农于耜劳止，生怠惰相，辍耕而游意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312337_comment'></div>行涧冈可五六里，至阿兰若，号曰珠溪，有小斋房，朴素幽洁，趺足而坐，松风可人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312337_comment'></div>住山老才作茶供已，即从座起而白予言：「我观世间，何者非幻，兹是陋室，强为我名」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312337_comment'></div>尔时秋崖告才老师：「但只恁么，于名何有」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312337_comment'></div>师大欢喜：「此即是名，名只恁么，无可不可，佛所说义，亦复如是」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312337_comment'></div>乃为作扁而说偈言：「是心如虚空，本自无一事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312337_comment'></div>若能只恁么，缘累从何生？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312337_comment'></div>而一切凡夫，不肯只恁么。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312337_comment'></div>妄生颠倒想，流浪五浊中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312337_comment'></div>见种种欲乐，炽然起贪痴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312337_comment'></div>无名着爱根，念念在富贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312337_comment'></div>由此一念故，戈矛生于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312337_comment'></div>犹如瘴毒蛇，竟日思噬齧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312337_comment'></div>又如彼阴贼，含沙而射人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312337_comment'></div>是人堕邪见，展转无是处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312337_comment'></div>我有一法门，非作亦非止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312337_comment'></div>粗茶与淡饭，直据现在身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312337_comment'></div>于十二时中，无复起妄想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312337_comment'></div>得安稳常住，不以苦为乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312337_comment'></div>如鹏与斥鴳，无适非逍遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312337_comment'></div>如鱼自潜深，不嗅钩上饵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312337_comment'></div>浮念一扫除，心逸而日休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312337_comment'></div>我今作是偈，付嘱于诸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1312337_comment'></div>能只恁么者，君子坦荡荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1312337_comment'></div>是名佛境界，安乐常欢喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1312337_comment'></div>不能只恁么，小人长戚戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1312337_comment'></div>是名魔境界，云何离垢缠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1312337_comment'></div>若人了此言，究竟渐净觉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1312337_comment'></div>淳祐四年三月望日。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1312337'></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1312337_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='325e9e4d6d12486eb3c36be6d56cd012_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("325e9e4d6d12486eb3c36be6d56cd012");'><span id='325e9e4d6d12486eb3c36be6d56cd012_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年</a>，52岁</div><div id='325e9e4d6d12486eb3c36be6d56cd012' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>方岳返里后为休宁吴竹洲（儆）后人吴元鼎（铉）作《友梅堂记》<div id='poem_1312339' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312339' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312339?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴元鼎友梅堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1249年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312339")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312339_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312339'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312339'>畴昔之夜，梦与客行溪谷间，沙清水寒，微霰暮集，有梅焉，苍皮半皴，偃蹇苔石，相与顾而乐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312339_comment'></div>客曰：「寒江苍苍，山月荒荒，侧倚崩崖，幽然自芳，非钓濑之严光乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312339_comment'></div>于君意何如」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312339_comment'></div>秋崖人曰：「高矣，抑未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312339_comment'></div>离世而立于独，薮泽处间而已矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312339_comment'></div>客曰：「天地既春，草木既津，憔悴惟腊，于涧之滨，非《离骚》经之灵均乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312339_comment'></div>于君意何如」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312339_comment'></div>秋崖人曰：「介矣，愈未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312339_comment'></div>非世而异于俗，枯槁赴渊而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312339_comment'></div>居，吾语子，吾将进子而易其观，可以希贤，可以作圣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312339_comment'></div>则指而谓之曰：「彼万仞立壁，烟昏雨寒，老色如铁，凛不可干，子盍观夫孟轲氏之岩岩？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312339_comment'></div>此颓櫩败瓦，野意萧疏，有美一人，雅澹冲虚，子盍观夫子颜子之如愚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312339_comment'></div>若然者，于子意又何如也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312339_comment'></div>语未既，有剥啄惊周公者，则东方白矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312339_comment'></div>秋崖人蹴樵青曰：「起扣门者非曩客也耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312339_comment'></div>窥之则竹洲后人讯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312339_comment'></div>君之言曰：「吾鄙在山林，无与从吾儿游者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312339_comment'></div>既择于梅使友之，作堂其间，以识吾训，子其为吾发焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312339_comment'></div>噫嘻，曩既与君言矣，欲为记者无以易是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312339_comment'></div>君其语而子资深，菊吾知其为隐者也，柴桑之遗民也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312339_comment'></div>莲吾知其为君子也，濂溪之老仙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312339_comment'></div>若人者，隐君子而非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312339_comment'></div>颜与孟丈人行也，而其友之云乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1312339_comment'></div>逢原勉之，毋或使玉立堂下者割管宁之席、作嵇康之书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1312339_comment'></div>竹洲后人曰吴铉元鼎，秋崖人曰方岳巨山，而是岁为淳祐之著雍涒滩云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1312339_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>方岳返里后为吴锡畴（字元伦）作《跋吴兄诗卷》<div id='poem_1312324' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312324' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312324?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋吴兄诗卷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1249年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312324")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312324_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312324'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312324'>予尝于何人卷中见左史公称「说著梅花定说君」之句，不知为竹洲后人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312324_comment'></div>意王恺之珊瑚扶疏二尺，美止此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312324_comment'></div>比贤君过予崖下，出其宝，则高三四尺者六七株，如「燕未成家寒食雨，人如中酒落花风」者尚多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312324_comment'></div>子其秘之，毋使豆粥韭蓱齑为帐下人所卖，彼恺辈者那得与君争长！</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1312324_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='b0051e8cf4fc40b5839709d4f10f2023_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b0051e8cf4fc40b5839709d4f10f2023");'><span id='b0051e8cf4fc40b5839709d4f10f2023_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年</a>，53岁</div><div id='b0051e8cf4fc40b5839709d4f10f2023' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>方岳赴任前作《题朱兄文（序）》<span class='inlineComment2'>（朱兄，指朱熹长孙朱鉴，字子明，官至湖广总领。）</span><div id='poem_1312315' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312315' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312315?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题朱兄文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1250年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312315")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312315_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312315'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312315'>晦庵诸孙访予秋崖下，适会昭武之役，不能烹伏雌为半日留，但相与苦话一顿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312315_comment'></div>因叹曰，夜来与泉使言，吾辈遂为世之狼籍人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312315_comment'></div>东边去撑触人了归，西边去撑触人了归，已自可笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312315_comment'></div>今日只与朋友谈文，又不能道妙道好，真狼籍人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312315_comment'></div>然竹坡喜诱进后辈，见诗即李、杜之，见文即欧、苏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312315_comment'></div>后辈不解其意，多是颠了，至有自号诗坛复古者，然则予狼籍人不狼籍矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312315_comment'></div>他日见竹坡，出予此纸，必抚手曰，前言戏之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312315_comment'></div>君归，尽取晦庵书读之，予无以赠君也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1312315_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>《小稿诗集》卷一七《次韵郑佥判》八首，其三有云：“衰鬓三千余太白，倦游五十二年是非”写于是年赴邵武前。（其三）<div id='poem_64352' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64352' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/64352?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵郑佥判<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1250年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_64352")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_64352_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_64352'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_64352'>渔村留得旧蓑衣，鹭侣鸥朋共断矶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_64352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_64352'>衰发三千馀丈白，倦游五十二年非。<div id='poem_sentence_1_64352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64352'>清风明月天四壁，老木苍藤草半扉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_64352'>寂寞相从交有道，骊驹未可遽言归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_64352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_64352'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_64352_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='e5d6d98a942c48bdbe349d3f5578a718_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e5d6d98a942c48bdbe349d3f5578a718");'><span id='e5d6d98a942c48bdbe349d3f5578a718_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1255')">1254-1255年</a>，57-58岁</div><div id='e5d6d98a942c48bdbe349d3f5578a718' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年</a>　在家闲居。《四库》本《秋崖集》词增录方岳《满庭芳·甲寅生日》，锡返里后冬作。<div id='poem_65105' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_65105' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/65105?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满庭芳 甲寅生日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1254年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_65105")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_65105_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_65105'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_65105'>雨带苍烟，须粘残雪，几年今日秋崖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_65105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_65105'>梅花篱落，不减旧情怀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_65105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_65105'>更觉神仙有分，一条冰、羽客官阶。<div id='poem_sentence_2_65105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_65105'>朝真外，研朱点易，风露滴松钗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_65105_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_65105'>蓬莱。<div id='poem_sentence_4_65105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_65105'>清浅未，吾将游戏，月坞云斋。<div id='poem_sentence_5_65105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_65105'>已相期汗漫，鹤蜕青鞋。<div id='poem_sentence_6_65105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_65105'>一念人间尘土，为雏孙、留醉茅柴。<div id='poem_sentence_7_65105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_65105'>今而后，村书杂字，仅有老生涯。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_65105_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年</a>　在家闲居。十一月，谢塈（与理宗有“椒房”之亲）来知徽州。《小稿》卷二二有《与谢少监》<div id='poem_1312021' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312021' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312021?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与谢少监劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1254年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312021")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312021_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312021'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312021'>某仰惟明执事佩二千石印绶，开府之初，百函而通爵里者纷如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312021_comment'></div>讲习不情之缪敬，揆时无用之空谈，亦既饫闻而厌听之矣，某敢略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312021_comment'></div>惟某祈下之鄙细人也，木石之与居，鹿豕之与游而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312021_comment'></div>诗不堪煮，起而糊其口于四方，乃以草茅不除，与世少可，所至撑触，往往炊不及熟而去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312021_comment'></div>盖自窃第奉常，于今二十又三年，计其在官不过五合六聚成七考耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312021_comment'></div>牛衣无恙，山林日长，每归田庐，一字不出柴荆外也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312021_comment'></div>如有明执事之至，仁声载涂，方将父母吾邦，而某则氓也，又奚其书之敢！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312021_comment'></div>谨自道其所以然者，具启事一通如左，惟戏下垂览焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1312021_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年</a>　在家闲居。《小稿》卷二五有《答郑提管》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年</a>　在家闲居。《小稿》卷二七有《转孙初生程弟有诗次韵时余直风适愈》，姑作于是年。知方岳有孙石外，另有孙名转。<div id='poem_64469' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64469' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/64469?labeling=true' target='_blank'>转孙初生程弟有诗次韵时予头风适愈</a><span class='authorDate'>（1254年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_64469")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_64469_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_64469'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_64469'>一庵深掩两三峰，白发从渠自不公。<div id='poem_sentence_0_64469_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_64469'>但有孙同开口笑，纵无檄亦愈头风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_64469_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64469'>鸢肩火色非吾事，牛背烟霏在眼中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64469_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_64469'>要识之无堪底用，归锄荷月且扶翁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_64469_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_64469'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_64469_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年</a>　在家闲居。作《朱氏六可堂记》<div id='poem_1312346' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312346' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312346?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朱氏六可堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1254年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312346")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312346_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312346'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312346'>《孝经》非纯圣人书，君家文公疑之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312346_comment'></div>不惟文公，致堂先生疑之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312346_comment'></div>不惟致堂，玉山先生疑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312346_comment'></div>至所谓六可者，则又裂取北宫文子道楚令尹围之言，文公笔而削之，固已在删去九十字之中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312346_comment'></div>君今掎以扁其堂而又属其记于予，得无家鸡之厌而野鹜之嗜与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312346_comment'></div>试尝与君慨想夫洙泗之上，神游乎孔、曾之间，亲见其穆然燕居，席间函丈，精聚神会，熙熙泰和，则尧舜禹之典谟具存，而伯夷、后夔之礼乐固无恙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312346_comment'></div>此其言行德义，容止进退，盖已粲然在目中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312346_comment'></div>故夫动容周旋之间，君子于是而观学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312346_comment'></div>孔子之所谓仁，不过视听言动之四；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312346_comment'></div>曾子之所谓道，不过容貌颜色辞气之三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312346_comment'></div>然则六可者，固学者用力涵养之地、主敬持守之则也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312346_comment'></div>君姑毋问其为汉先儒之训诂、唐开元之章句，而以夫之六言者就其所谓可，去其所谓不可，则一贯之指，不言已传，六可不在忠恕乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312346_comment'></div>自任之重，死而后已，六可不在宏毅乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312346_comment'></div>好修者三省，自得者一唯，曾何人哉，希之则是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312346_comment'></div>君名某，经略公之诸孙，徽文公之族子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312346_comment'></div>予虽未识其人，而能作堂储书，以夫之六言诏厥后，其斯亦可书矣，于是乎书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312346_comment'></div>宝祐甲寅除日，里人方岳记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1312346_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年</a>　在家闲居。作《跋赵兄诗卷》<div id='poem_1312321' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312321' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312321?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋赵兄诗卷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1254年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312321")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312321_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312321'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312321'>予非知诗人，赵公迫而与言诗，过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312321_comment'></div>然予观世之学晚唐者不必读书，但彷佛其声嗽便觉优孟似孙叔敖，掇皮皆真，予每叹恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312321_comment'></div>夫晚唐之不昌也，君其肯之，则以吾之不可学柳下惠之可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312321_comment'></div>宝祐甲寅良月中休，秋崖方某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1312321_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年</a>　在家闲居。作《跋李君蜀议》<div id='poem_1312318' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312318' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312318?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋李君蜀议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1254年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312318")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312318_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312318'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312318'>「汉骑城夔仲谋惧，艾毡入剑孙吴平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312318_comment'></div>素船倒峡长江一，昶俘入朝江南下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312318_comment'></div>无蜀则无吴，李君之论伟矣，然犹是余毅夫未入蜀前议论耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312318_comment'></div>前救败棋之着固应尔，今日活死棋之着当何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312318_comment'></div>王积薪辈几无措手处矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312318_comment'></div>使遇骊山老母，必自别有一着。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312318_comment'></div>宝祐二闰廿二方某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1312318_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年</a>　在家闲居，改知饶州，辞不就。《小稿》卷五《申省乞祠》及《又申》表明其不愿出仕之意已绝。作品：《申省乞祠》、《又申》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年2月</a>　在家闲居，改知饶州，辞不就。二月董槐为右相兼枢密使。方岳作《与董丞相》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《小稿》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1311951' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311951' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311951?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与董丞相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1255年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311951")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311951_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311951'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311951'>某仰惟岩廊峻极，礼绝百僚，下土虮虱之微，惟有屏息，岂敢以凡笔陋墨尘滓太清！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311951_comment'></div>而山林之日长，未尝得望符采，平生本末有不得不略陈于宰衡之下，惟钧慈其垂听焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311951_comment'></div>某起于草茅，与世落落，在督府则以忤同幕归，在庐山则以怒邻梱徙，在邵武则以劾巡属罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311951_comment'></div>某虽至愚，亦岂欲其至此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311951_comment'></div>性有倖直之累，学无涵养之功，执而不通，每每妄发，然亦不过争公事耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311951_comment'></div>独邵武之斥，有足慨叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311951_comment'></div>属邑建宁县因有追胥峒顽群辈而劫敚之，敢弄锄梃，某既绳治，随已帖息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311951_comment'></div>推原本始，则一小小寄居实为囊橐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311951_comment'></div>某以为此而不治乱也，乃具按劾，不知何者章格不下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311951_comment'></div>某非才守垒如此，则何颜以见吏民？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311951_comment'></div>自劾归田，得请而罢，一斥不复，五年于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311951_comment'></div>中间当国者履斋擢之进士第，座主也，独此荐为文字官，知己也，然犹自信薄命，未尝敢有非意之干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311951_comment'></div>乃今天地开除，真儒柱石，某徒为耕夫耘子相贺于田，而光范无某之三黜，翘材无某之一迹，某虽欲囿于陶铸，其不惧谴斥而辄有请耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311951_comment'></div>不图赞化之初，亦在起废之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311951_comment'></div>恭惟此意，对越在天，古风寂寥，忽见今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311951_comment'></div>某谨具启事一通，惟经纶之暇略赐览观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311951_comment'></div>某老矣无能，非以受恩为喜，而以受知为喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311951_comment'></div>盖不请而与之，虽万钟之重，于造化为大公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311951_comment'></div>不请而得之，虽一介之微，于么么为大荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1311951_comment'></div>不腆芜陋之辞，固非为己私谢，而为天下贺也，某而后知所归矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1311951_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年2月</a>　在家闲居，改知饶州，辞不就。作《与丘文昌》，追言其罢邵武情状甚详。<div id='poem_1311993' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311993' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311993?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与丘文昌劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1255年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311993")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311993_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311993'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311993'>某辱在门墙，于今馀二十年，豹尾神旗，建号大梱，草庐耕凿，适隶二天，岂不愿依倚末光，壮此流落！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311993_comment'></div>而山林屏废之迹，渔樵疏散之人，固不能奉咫尺书以自附于门籍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311993_comment'></div>伏惟育人材如《诗》菁莪，拔汇征如《易》茅茹，闻某此言，必将动心焉，而奚其逋慢之罪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311993_comment'></div>恃此无恐，有如青天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311993_comment'></div>某一斥五年，不复知有人间事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311993_comment'></div>里人有广德倅刘姓而骐其名者，苦欲介一书于辕和，某辞之不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311993_comment'></div>刘君自太学取高科垂三十年，甫得副簉，斯亦可念也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311993_comment'></div>敢告先生，泽之以霖雨之手，包之以云梦之胸，如某受赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311993_comment'></div>某不自抑畏，辄敢为一布之，惟先生之函盖也而恕其僭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1311993_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年2月</a>　在家闲居，改知饶州，辞不就。程元凤权工部尚书，签书枢密院事，权参加政事。方岳作《与程尚书》<div id='poem_1311988' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311988' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311988?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与程尚书劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1255年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311988")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311988_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311988'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311988'>某惟吾乡诸老不登政事堂者有年于此矣，明公清忠粹学，主知日隆，犹以柱下为执法之官，不若近侍论思之密勿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311988_comment'></div>涣发大号，四方颙颙跂而望之，莫甚于耕野之老，盖以明公一日登政事，则前日之所取而荐进者，吾今自陶成之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311988_comment'></div>然则某之贺也，上以为天子贺，下以贺其私也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1311988_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年</a>　在家闲居，改知饶州，辞不就。《小稿诗集》卷一九《元日雨》二首均写于是年正月初一。二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《小稿》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_64248' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64248' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/64248?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元日雨<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1255年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_64248")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_64248_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_64248'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_64248'>那得工夫作往还，一犁取日破荒湾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_64248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_64248'>春今又绿山中草，酒不能朱镜里颜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_64248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64248'>六十只馀三岁在，百年亦是霎时间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_64248'>村村雨色冥濛外，已觉天公露一斑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_64248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_64248'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_64248_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_64249' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64249' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/64249?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1255年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_64249_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_64249'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_64249'>云泥隔断拜年人，天自怜予老病身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_64249_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_64249'>荠菜共挑元日雨，梅花未放去年春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_64249_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64249'>风烟不尽惟吾老，造化无他只此仁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64249_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_64249'>小试园林栽接手，山中亦是一洪钧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_64249_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_64249'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_64249_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年</a>　在家闲居，改知饶州，辞不就。婺源友人滕和书见过，为作《尚书大意序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（滕和书，名证，著名理学家滕琳子，方岳少时同窗。）</span><div id='poem_1312287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312287?labeling=true' target='_blank'>滕和叔尚书大意序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1255年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312287")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312287_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312287'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312287'>吾州以经名家者多矣，《书》为最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312287_comment'></div>以《书》名家者加多矣，滕为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312287_comment'></div>《书》自程文昌、王大监皆有所论著，天下所谓程泰之《禹贡图志》、王晦叔《尚书小传》者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312287_comment'></div>至溪斋先生与其弟合淝令君同登晦翁之门，学者谓之新安两滕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312287_comment'></div>和叔渐涵于二父之渊源，披剥于百家之林薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312287_comment'></div>盖自与予别三十有五年矣，一日访予崖底，出其所著书曰《尚书大意》者十二万言，教予曰：「子亦知夫凡书之有大意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312287_comment'></div>犹之木焉，本而非节目也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312287_comment'></div>犹之水焉，源而非派别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312287_comment'></div>若《书》之大意，则一中字而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312287_comment'></div>允执厥中，《书》所以始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312287_comment'></div>咸中有庆，《书》所以终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312287_comment'></div>以此一字，读此一书，迎刃解矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312287_comment'></div>予受而读之，既请曰：「以中为《书》之大意，吾未之前闻也，子于何有所闻」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312287_comment'></div>曰：「予闻之先君子，先君子闻之紫阳翁，紫阳翁闻之濂洛诸老，而予发其秘者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312287_comment'></div>宝祐乙卯重阳日，友人方岳谨序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1312287_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年</a>　在家闲居，改知饶州，辞不就。为歙人汪正己（曾任管辖）作《竹所主人所藏余诗》<div id='poem_1312296' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312296' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312296?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋竹所主人所藏余诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1255年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312296")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312296_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312296'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312296'>竹所主人谓汪君正己也，其师面目严冷，出语辄撑触人，君每每以乐易左右之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312296_comment'></div>属闻其师亡，为藏剑履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312296_comment'></div>闻政山能使其徒竭力无几微见于颜面，此李将军不击刁斗法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312296_comment'></div>李广、程不识皆为汉名将，然士卒苦不识而乐从广，吾未知其孰是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312296_comment'></div>君归，见所中青士问之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1312296_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='7f9185dd12a84c69b1e782e534c482c3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7f9185dd12a84c69b1e782e534c482c3");'><span id='7f9185dd12a84c69b1e782e534c482c3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>，59岁</div><div id='7f9185dd12a84c69b1e782e534c482c3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年7月</a>　在家闲居。起知宁国府，未上，罢。改知袁州（江西宜春），七月，蔡抗参知政事。《小稿》卷七有《通蔡总郎》，卷二二有《与蔡编修》作品：《通蔡总郎》、《与蔡编修》<div id='poem_1311688' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311688' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311688?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代通蔡总郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311688")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311688_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311688'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311688'>伏以蜚声斗北，烂其郎宿之晖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311688_comment'></div>出宰江东，幸甚使天之近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311688_comment'></div>敢于传鲤，告以视龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311688_comment'></div>伏念某汗青者流，副墨之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311688_comment'></div>窥诸父词林之根柢，何碌碌未有奇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311688_comment'></div>藉一官家世之蔓延，宁郁郁久居此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311688_comment'></div>虽张仪之舌在，岂虞翻之骨屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311688_comment'></div>粤自落南，极知计左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311688_comment'></div>挟书册于关雪岭云之外，化衣襟以蛮烟瘴雨之腥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311688_comment'></div>方与庾梅而别归，又为陶柳而驱去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311688_comment'></div>思昔中牟之化，今已在七不堪之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311688_comment'></div>正复阳城之生，亦付之六太息而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311688_comment'></div>过不自料，勇为此来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311688_comment'></div>安知债邑之穷，介在丛山之底。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311688_comment'></div>厥土刚燥，岁无万宝之穰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311688_comment'></div>其民焦熬，家乏百金之殖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311688_comment'></div>盖凛然其掣肘，亦何为乎折腰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311688_comment'></div>独以鹪鹩之一枝，适览凤凰于千仞，则其依向，讵不切深！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311688_comment'></div>恭惟某官，以中郎人物之宗，传魁省文章之印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1311688_comment'></div>所谓有是父有是子，郁然歆、向之家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1311688_comment'></div>其将使吾君使吾民，盛于尧舜之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1311688_comment'></div>有美三衢之颂，略如两汉之循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1311688_comment'></div>民方佩犊而带牛，时或鸣狐而啸鼠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1311688_comment'></div>曰司直吾父母，至则息潢池之兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1311688_comment'></div>观而曹皆乡邻，岂欲为绿林之盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1311688_comment'></div>夺情而起，革面如携，于此见信之及豚鱼，亦焉用威之以貔虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1311688_comment'></div>是为素蕴，上所深知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1311688_comment'></div>若然则出总于军储，夫岂惟有事于边圉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1311688_comment'></div>侯谁在矣，未尝不叹，曰江左之有夷吾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1311688_comment'></div>迟之几何，亦将相戒，以中国之相司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1311688_comment'></div>某靖言绵薄，惟恐锦伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1311688_comment'></div>保障乎茧丝乎，择斯二者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1311688_comment'></div>山岳也河海也，孰能一之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1311688_comment'></div>尚邀福于前人，亦有辞于永世。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1311688_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1311985' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311985' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311985?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与蔡编修劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311985")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311985_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311985'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311985'>某脱襫袯起民伍中，朝士之相知者落如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311985_comment'></div>独明执事一见辄器许之，若将以为可与驱驰斯世者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311985_comment'></div>而不知其愚戆疏直，与人枘凿，适可着之颓檐败瓦下耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311985_comment'></div>始某为督枢招致，方日日诣府辞行，不暇与明执事道心曲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311985_comment'></div>不得已来此，无几何日矣，辄忽忽不乐，自度无一事可为报效，盖尝束担径归田矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311985_comment'></div>督枢不以为罪，挽留之再三，今又西行边，某谊不可不告而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311985_comment'></div>重以老妻疽作于背，姑谒告以俟其还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311985_comment'></div>读执事兴怀当世之书，三复感叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311985_comment'></div>自此山深林密，无相见期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311985_comment'></div>田家作劳，或与黄犊对眠时，不能不一思高致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311985_comment'></div>某临纸惘然。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1311985_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
滁州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='801c12186b9a4e55ba8f5a623acd3cc8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("801c12186b9a4e55ba8f5a623acd3cc8");'><span id='801c12186b9a4e55ba8f5a623acd3cc8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1234&endYear=1234')">1234年</a>，37岁</div><div id='801c12186b9a4e55ba8f5a623acd3cc8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1234&endYear=1234')">1234年</a>　方岳丁母忧，服阙，调滁州教授，结识赵葵。按：岳于秋冬间到任，作《通权教蔡佥判》。是年，理宗启用真德秀、魏了翁等道学家，号称“小元祐”。自此理学兴盛。岳为赵葵作《代贺魏（工部）侍郎》。方岳伯兄荐为第五，岳为作《代汪表侄谢启》、《代大兄谢启》。作品：《通权教蔡佥判》、《代贺魏（工部）侍郎》、《代汪表侄谢启》、《代大兄谢启》<div id='poem_1311696' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311696' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311696?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通权教蔡佥判启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1234年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311696")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311696_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311696'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311696'>伏以挹芝眉于鹤府，曾论师学之同；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311696_comment'></div>扬木舌于鳣堂，式借宾僚之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311696_comment'></div>得君为代，告我以情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311696_comment'></div>盖将绸缪朋友之交，其必脱略世俗之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311696_comment'></div>云胡不喜，久已相知，恭惟某官，得中郎之异书，摛君谟之妙墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311696_comment'></div>尝袖《周官》而独往，岂惟识河汾王氏之传；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311696_comment'></div>欲起汉儒而与言，当尽得洙泗圣门之蕴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311696_comment'></div>方其披琅玕以叫阊阖，谓且跨元圃而登昆崙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311696_comment'></div>奚为环滁山水之间，肯寻欧阳文字之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311696_comment'></div>依芙蓉于俭幕，漫穿从事之衫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311696_comment'></div>采芹藻于鲁宫，每重博士之席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311696_comment'></div>于以见斯文之寄，其或舍吾曹而谁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311696_comment'></div>遄有茧函，置之渠观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311696_comment'></div>某粤从雨别，坐想风期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311696_comment'></div>思昔老先生，几眼空于四海；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311696_comment'></div>每评诸弟子，仅齿及于数人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311696_comment'></div>顾惟见收于奔北之馀，亦曾未快其图南之适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311696_comment'></div>推一夔于别省，鸡失旦而始鸣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311696_comment'></div>侪八恺于甲科，鸿遇风而犹却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1311696_comment'></div>孰为幸会，辱在交承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1311696_comment'></div>有嘉益友之分深，敢叹广文之官冷！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1311696_comment'></div>山行六七里，想未寒鸥鹭之盟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1311696_comment'></div>云飞九万程，恐莫企鹍鹏之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1311696_comment'></div>愿闻一语，谨已三熏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1311696_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1311811' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311811' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311811?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代贺魏侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1234年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311811")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311811_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311811'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311811'>伏审涣扬书赞，进贰宪曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311811_comment'></div>民自得于湖山，久奏吴门之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311811_comment'></div>帝慨思于人物，趣归汉殿之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311811_comment'></div>期得祥刑，斯皇殊綍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311811_comment'></div>某不胜燕贺，敢后鱼传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311811_comment'></div>致治几成康，坐想措刑之盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311811_comment'></div>使君为尧舜，谅怀济世之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311811_comment'></div>无斁颂言，切惟监在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311811_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1311811_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1311699' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311699' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311699?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代汪表侄谢解启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1234年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311699")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311699_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311699'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311699'>伏以圣天子新端平之政，饬士习者再三；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311699_comment'></div>乡大夫登贤能之书，推礼乐于第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311699_comment'></div>凛有卢前之愧，喜无牛后之嘲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311699_comment'></div>何德堪之，为倖多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311699_comment'></div>试尝谓士生尧舜之世，谁不欲身致晁董之科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311699_comment'></div>矧惟琴瑟之更张，岂复笙竽之杂袭！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311699_comment'></div>风飞雷厉，汉札十行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311699_comment'></div>地辟天开，唐文一变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311699_comment'></div>乃酌计偕之额，聿回儒学之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311699_comment'></div>于然而来，卓乎其杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311699_comment'></div>犹共逐中原之鹿，人人自谓得之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311699_comment'></div>至独为前列之龟，区区秪有惭耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311699_comment'></div>顾如某者，仅若而人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311699_comment'></div>结发从诸公游，窃考太平之典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311699_comment'></div>束书有四方志，愿为君子之儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311699_comment'></div>虽极知文举之才疏，未易诋洛阳之年少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311699_comment'></div>一灯夜雪，两战秋风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311699_comment'></div>思昔故家，起龙鱼而洗日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311699_comment'></div>繄我季父，有雕鹗之在天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1311699_comment'></div>寥乎相业之无传，幸而书种之不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1311699_comment'></div>贾予馀勇，与众先登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1311699_comment'></div>孰云扬秕之前，或叹穿杨之巧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1311699_comment'></div>邑有故事，人多诵言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1311699_comment'></div>谓畴昔当甲午之元，尝魁北斗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1311699_comment'></div>以《春秋》无己亥之误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1311699_comment'></div>遄冠南宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1311699_comment'></div>意其气数之循环，俾此功名之破的。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1311699_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇蜀文翁之教化，今韩愈之声光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1311699_comment'></div>抉云汉分天章，涵浸诗书之泽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1311699_comment'></div>呈琅玕叫阊阖，醲薰翰墨之香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1311699_comment'></div>言观才屈、宋而道羲、黄，将使家皋、夔而人稷、契，玉我文明之治，锵然熙洽之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1311699_comment'></div>有嘉燕凝，不知螽跃，迄致辽东之献，亦空冀北之群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1311699_comment'></div>某敢不连拔茅之征，乘破竹之势！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1311699_comment'></div>乌之鸷累百数而不如鹗，已先雌伏之卑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1311699_comment'></div>鲲之大几千里而化为鹏，遄借雄风之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1311699_comment'></div>丹衷所属，赤牍奚殚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1311699_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1311700' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311700' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311700?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代大兄谢解启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1234年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 ·
