</span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311700")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311700_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311700'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311700'>伏以雁行别省，谬推李广之无双；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311700_comment'></div>鹗荐计台，乃寘牧之于第五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311700_comment'></div>事有出于偶尔，人或谓之当然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311700_comment'></div>虽未信月评之是非，亦姑免秋风之寥落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311700_comment'></div>尝谓文章虽有定价，然而场屋特其假涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311700_comment'></div>历观隋唐以来问学之卑，窃叹晁董而有科举之累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311700_comment'></div>波流之漫，风靡以从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311700_comment'></div>至今日而谓之时文，岂圣门所望于儒者！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311700_comment'></div>吁几年于此矣，谁一洗而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311700_comment'></div>如某者闻道最迂，识字可数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311700_comment'></div>悲歌长铗，饱谙世路之涛澜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311700_comment'></div>痴守短檠，倦听雪楼之钟鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311700_comment'></div>尝抚《周官》而太息，欲起汉儒而有言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311700_comment'></div>其如文闱哇陋之为，不过书生呫毕而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311700_comment'></div>乃难入筝琶之耳，已久寒笔砚之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311700_comment'></div>科宁有利不利耶，奚必南之燕而北之粤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311700_comment'></div>时所谓可则可耳，岂真愚于虞而智于秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311700_comment'></div>幸而见收，诚不自意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311700_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇鲠论子方之家世，丽藻子西之典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1311700_comment'></div>骢马退朝，共骇铁冠之御史；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1311700_comment'></div>木牛流运，誓安井络之边民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1311700_comment'></div>言观才屈宋而道羲黄，且欲家皋夔而人稷契，玉我文明之治，锵然熙洽之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1311700_comment'></div>有伟会盟，适为座主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1311700_comment'></div>乃贾挥毫之勇，迄今换骨而仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1311700_comment'></div>某敢不绪缉所闻，激越其志！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1311700_comment'></div>独惭两宋，弟不可以先之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1311700_comment'></div>要有一韩，敌自为之惊耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1311700_comment'></div>勉旃行矣，当亦褎然。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1311700_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
安徽
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a8770b2752fb4095b55e32144a61dba2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a8770b2752fb4095b55e32144a61dba2");'><span id='a8770b2752fb4095b55e32144a61dba2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=-100000&endYear=1235')">1235年</a>，38岁</div><div id='a8770b2752fb4095b55e32144a61dba2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年</a>　方岳任滁州教授，寻除淮东安抚司干官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年</a>　方岳任滁州教授，寻除淮东安抚司干官。是年蒙军大举南侵，淮、蜀、京、襄皆紧。方岳于《次韵酬章教授》述其治事甚详，且知其于受命制干后（六月）即赴南徐（镇江）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年7月</a>　方岳平定高邮军哄事（方岳《后义倡传》有记载）。且据方岳词《望江南·乙未生日》注知：方岳于平定高邮军哄事后，始返滁州携眷再来南徐。全子才、刘子澄坐唐州之役弃兵宵盾，各削二秩。时均为赵葵下属。方岳稿中有《别子才司令》诗和《满庭芳·寿刘参议》词。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年</a>　二月，真德秀参知政事，五月薨。十月，参知政事魏了翁同签枢院事，力辞，不允。《小稿》卷二二《与魏参政》及《祭魏参政》（文）知，方岳当于是年冬会魏于镇江。<div id='poem_1312379' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312379' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312379?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭魏参政文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1235年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312379")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312379_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312379'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312379'>呜呼，蜀自三苏公不作，于今几何年兮，予尝意其水恧而山羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312379_comment'></div>天地之秘宝韬光铲彩，郁屈而不平兮，故其发也勃焉，而有斐君子特立于西州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312379_comment'></div>学探邃古之奥，文洗时俗之陋，而浩然于胸中者自一宇宙兮，盖蹴训诂之圃而姬孔之与游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312379_comment'></div>以其精微者治身，以其粗浅者治世，是心固将尧舜吾君民兮，而不知一苇杭之，何以障百川于横流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312379_comment'></div>彼谁其秉国之均，如重阴且霾，日月为之晦冥兮，而矫然独鹤之嘹唳，乃欲空百鸟之喧啾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312379_comment'></div>抱遗经于荒遐之裔，乐斯道于寂寞之滨者，与岁月而相忘兮，亦既筑山房于白鹤之麓，而眠云卧雪，吟风醉月，侃侃乎其无物外之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312379_comment'></div>但遨嬉于翰墨之林，而秦篆汉籀流落人间者，太山一毫芒兮，至其妙于心，则伏羲以前之《大易》，而笔于书，则获麟以后之《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312379_comment'></div>忽云翳之划开，豁中天之大夜，下尺一趣诸老以来归兮，人固以为适当太平之期，愿观德化之成，而众君子之聚在本朝者，殆将人稷契而身伊周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312379_comment'></div>历观近岁诸贤之志，各欲出其力以救斯世之沦胥兮，而彼苍者天，岂其不欲平治耶，胡驾言中道而摧辀！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312379_comment'></div>西山其颓，而天目之老、晋陵之魁亦相继而凋落兮，独吾白鹤山人在，而且犹旁睨如棋之局、孤閒横水之舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312379_comment'></div>然庶几其可以系中外之望，以待天人之定兮，而复乘云气，骑箕尾，渺松江以上征，而不为苍生其小留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312379_comment'></div>畴昔之夜，谒公南徐，曰众欢之不可息而予亦信以为然兮，及今见之，则嘅叹其为李西平之子，而嘉奖其为异于臧宫、马武之俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312379_comment'></div>人生倾意气耳，故今闻公之丧，昼喟而夜吁兮，而况朝失元老，士失宗儒，其将付斯世于悠悠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312379_comment'></div>乃作白鹤之些曰：白鹤飞兮山之幽，梳雪羽兮风飕飕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312379_comment'></div>时不与兮吾谁尤，白鹤归兮河之洲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312379_comment'></div>苏台杳兮云正愁，唳华表兮天知否。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1312379_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年</a>　方岳作《次韵范侍郎（钟）寄赵校正》，盖写于是年六月以前，时仍任教滁州。<div id='poem_64833' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64833' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/64833?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵范侍郎寄赵校正</a><span class='authorDate'>（1235年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_64833")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_64833_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_64833'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_64833'>呜呼小雅废，边角摇军声。<div id='poem_sentence_0_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_64833'>采芹旧青衿，亦须事力征。<div id='poem_sentence_1_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64833'>朱轓挟武将，白眼轻儒生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_64833'>区区众浊间，嗟子难为清。<div id='poem_sentence_3_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_64833'>向来意何如，岂惟以文鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_4_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_64833'>乃今事大谬，老气犹峥嵘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_64833'>论事抉石猊，摛辞吸川鲸。<div id='poem_sentence_6_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_64833'>久抱一束书，空山卧月明。<div id='poem_sentence_7_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_64833'>窃忧蠢诐胡，鳞介腥神京。<div id='poem_sentence_8_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_64833'>幸存三寸舌，宁守二尺檠。<div id='poem_sentence_9_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_64833'>有愚欲献璞，无意望报琼。<div id='poem_sentence_10_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_64833'>云何山阴兴，莫写塞下情。<div id='poem_sentence_11_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_64833'>竹床撼夜柝，茅屋荒秋城。<div id='poem_sentence_12_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_64833'>回首阊阖门，何啻九万程。<div id='poem_sentence_13_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_64833'>愿言大白低，滁山足春耕。<div id='poem_sentence_14_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_64833'>堂皇坐醉翁，开閤延群英。<div id='poem_sentence_15_64833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_64833'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_64833_comment'></div></div></div><br />年份未详　王迈知徽州，是年郡人李以申作《新安续志》。歙人郑江（郑省仓）进士及第。丘岳知真州（仪征）有战功，进为淮东提刑。方岳作《水调歌头·寿丘提刑》颂之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《小稿》（卷一））</span><div id='poem_65103' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_65103' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/65103?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>寿丘提刑</a><span class='authorDate'>（5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_65103")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_65103_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_65103'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_65103'>甓社有明月，夜半吐光寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_65103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_65103'>淮南草木飞动，秀出斗牛间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_65103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_65103'>自有秦沙以后，试问少游而下，谁捲入毫端。<div id='poem_sentence_2_65103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_65103'>补衮仲山甫，冰雪照云寰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_65103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_65103'>霄汉近，绣衣去，锦衣还。<div id='poem_sentence_4_65103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_65103'>江南且为梅醉，莫道岁将阑。<div id='poem_sentence_5_65103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_65103'>三百六旬欲换，五百岁终才始，日月两循环。<div id='poem_sentence_6_65103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_65103'>酌彼金错落，浇此碧琅玕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_65103_comment'></div></div></div><br />年份未详　赐少师特进银青光禄大夫赵方谥忠肃。方岳为赵范、赵葵代作《赵忠肃赐谥谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《小稿》（卷一））</span><div id='poem_1311606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赵忠肃赐谥谢表<span class='inlineComment2'>（以下代赵相公）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311606")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311606'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311606'>星霜代谢，未忘没世之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311606_comment'></div>云汉昭回，遄举易名之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311606_comment'></div>感恩之渥，有涕其滂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311606_comment'></div>伏念臣先臣某，起自诸生，久膺繁使，誓欲捐糜于昭代，实繇遭际于先皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311606_comment'></div>凡闑外制将军，曾微掣肘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311606_comment'></div>傥舟中为敌国，安所容身！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311606_comment'></div>以故十年无敌骑之窥边，四境谓老熊之当道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311606_comment'></div>乃莫返长沙之舍，已怀鵩赋之忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311606_comment'></div>至今登岘山之巅，或堕羊碑之泪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311606_comment'></div>痛营屯于细柳，共尸祝于亢桑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311606_comment'></div>于赫旌题，聿严庙貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311606_comment'></div>木其拱矣，尚兴当馈之思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311606_comment'></div>谥而诔之，肆及漏泉之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311606_comment'></div>此盖恭遇皇帝陛下，励精新政，拊髀旧臣，永惟华衮之褒，荣甚凌烟之画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311606_comment'></div>臣教忠之言在耳，移孝之志填膺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311606_comment'></div>北命吉甫而南南仲，常负前茅之恨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311606_comment'></div>生走仲达而死诸葛，尚邀横草之知。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1311606_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6374c77a3c424fd6942d3ed2676e89c4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6374c77a3c424fd6942d3ed2676e89c4");'><span id='6374c77a3c424fd6942d3ed2676e89c4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1238')">1236-1238年</a>，39-41岁</div><div id='6374c77a3c424fd6942d3ed2676e89c4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年5月</a>　赵葵进华文阁直学士，方岳为作《代谢除华文阁直学士》（《小稿》卷八）<div id='poem_1311704' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311704' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311704?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代谢除华文阁直学士启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1236年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311704")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311704_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311704'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311704'>分梱边城，蔑闻治状；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311704_comment'></div>进班邃阁，猥玷除书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311704_comment'></div>盖恳切而牢辞者凡六章，其趑趄而未遑者馀半载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311704_comment'></div>终莫回于成涣，亦窃虑于渎蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311704_comment'></div>虽李广数奇，正不羡侯于校尉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311704_comment'></div>然汲黯妄发，或疑敢薄于淮阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311704_comment'></div>早夜以思，进退维谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311704_comment'></div>正恐酬恩之无所，复虞留令之有诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311704_comment'></div>宜贬而褒，以荣为惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311704_comment'></div>伏念某马齿加长，鼯技已穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311704_comment'></div>王事靡盬，不遑启处，报国之心犹铁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311704_comment'></div>王事多难，维其棘矣，忧时之发欲银。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311704_comment'></div>旋观兵气之缠，可骇旄头之彗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311704_comment'></div>孰御强邻之见逼，尺土皆安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311704_comment'></div>盍来群策以防秋，寸阴是惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311704_comment'></div>今乃脉络之不贯，安得精神之自强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311704_comment'></div>内阻外讧，事已至此；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311704_comment'></div>朝奏暮报，人尚迟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311704_comment'></div>胡为书檄之交驰，竟令岁月之虚老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1311704_comment'></div>思虑所及，梦寐亦惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1311704_comment'></div>若然则进直于西清，亦奚以少宽于北顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1311704_comment'></div>言观纶綍，有腼缙绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1311704_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇妙造化之权，公刑赏之柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1311704_comment'></div>陈十事以坚帝意，首及人材；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1311704_comment'></div>有一德以享天心，力扶世运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1311704_comment'></div>进言之暇，劝上勿遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1311704_comment'></div>使非意之侥踰，迄不容于控避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1311704_comment'></div>某已上丐骸之请，难忘刻骨之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1311704_comment'></div>一夫向隅为主忧，岂敢怀于畎亩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1311704_comment'></div>四郊多垒则臣辱，慨徒死于封疆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1311704_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年6月</a>　刑部尚书兼侍读洪咨夔卒。前此方岳有《回洪侍郎》文。又，为胡显作《代谢除军器监簿》。有酬戴式之三首。《小稿诗集》载。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年</a>　七月，以赵范失襄城，罪重罚轻，诏罢职奉祠。八月，诏更削两秩，谪居建宁（建瓯）府，方岳作书曲为宽解。少挺多东西！！！！作品：《代诸监司与庙堂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（是年，郑清之、乔行简二相策免。方岳有《贺许兵书》。是年，歙人方回十岁。）</span><div id='poem_1311941' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311941' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311941?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代诸监司与庙堂书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1236年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311941")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311941_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311941'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311941'>某等不避诛夷，辄殚恳切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311941_comment'></div>某等闻吴公玠为裨将时，世固未知名也，而刘公子羽独奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311941_comment'></div>其后刘公守兴元，萨里罕之兵奄至，兴元失守，刘公仅以身免，朝廷责散官安置白州，吴公至纳节以赎，而刘公卒得为有宋名臣，国史书之，闻者兴起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311941_comment'></div>盖以必罚者朝廷之公法也，相友者天下之大义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311941_comment'></div>公法在朝廷，则诛戮窜殛，一毫不可以轻贷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311941_comment'></div>大义在天下，则哀鸣救解，虽赴汤蹈火有不可辞者，而况官秩云乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311941_comment'></div>某等辱知于前荆湖制使赵尚书，盖不啻吴公玠之于刘公子羽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311941_comment'></div>今尚书公不幸有子羽之罪，而某等不能为玠之所为，则不负知己而羞当世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311941_comment'></div>尚书力却数十万强敌于襄樊之围，斯亦难已，而变起于不虞，祻生于所玩，萧墙之内，枭獍骤兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311941_comment'></div>事至于此，固已无可言者，抑太史公所谓「身虽陷败，然其所摧败亦足暴于天下」，吁可悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311941_comment'></div>某等不胜区区之请，辄以闻奏，欲各纳三官以赎尚书公之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311941_comment'></div>伏惟圣君贤相天地并包，特屈刑章，俾从末减，如此则尚书未死之日，犹有勉思报国之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311941_comment'></div>不然，某等恐其函羞九原，长不瞑目矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311941_comment'></div>情迫辞急，惟钧慈其垂情焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1311941_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年3月</a>　魏了翁卒，年六十。方岳作《祭魏参政》<div id='poem_1312379' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312379' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312379?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭魏参政文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1235年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312379")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312379_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312379'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312379'>呜呼，蜀自三苏公不作，于今几何年兮，予尝意其水恧而山羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312379_comment'></div>天地之秘宝韬光铲彩，郁屈而不平兮，故其发也勃焉，而有斐君子特立于西州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312379_comment'></div>学探邃古之奥，文洗时俗之陋，而浩然于胸中者自一宇宙兮，盖蹴训诂之圃而姬孔之与游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312379_comment'></div>以其精微者治身，以其粗浅者治世，是心固将尧舜吾君民兮，而不知一苇杭之，何以障百川于横流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312379_comment'></div>彼谁其秉国之均，如重阴且霾，日月为之晦冥兮，而矫然独鹤之嘹唳，乃欲空百鸟之喧啾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312379_comment'></div>抱遗经于荒遐之裔，乐斯道于寂寞之滨者，与岁月而相忘兮，亦既筑山房于白鹤之麓，而眠云卧雪，吟风醉月，侃侃乎其无物外之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312379_comment'></div>但遨嬉于翰墨之林，而秦篆汉籀流落人间者，太山一毫芒兮，至其妙于心，则伏羲以前之《大易》，而笔于书，则获麟以后之《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312379_comment'></div>忽云翳之划开，豁中天之大夜，下尺一趣诸老以来归兮，人固以为适当太平之期，愿观德化之成，而众君子之聚在本朝者，殆将人稷契而身伊周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312379_comment'></div>历观近岁诸贤之志，各欲出其力以救斯世之沦胥兮，而彼苍者天，岂其不欲平治耶，胡驾言中道而摧辀！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312379_comment'></div>西山其颓，而天目之老、晋陵之魁亦相继而凋落兮，独吾白鹤山人在，而且犹旁睨如棋之局、孤閒横水之舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312379_comment'></div>然庶几其可以系中外之望，以待天人之定兮，而复乘云气，骑箕尾，渺松江以上征，而不为苍生其小留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312379_comment'></div>畴昔之夜，谒公南徐，曰众欢之不可息而予亦信以为然兮，及今见之，则嘅叹其为李西平之子，而嘉奖其为异于臧宫、马武之俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312379_comment'></div>人生倾意气耳，故今闻公之丧，昼喟而夜吁兮，而况朝失元老，士失宗儒，其将付斯世于悠悠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312379_comment'></div>乃作白鹤之些曰：白鹤飞兮山之幽，梳雪羽兮风飕飕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312379_comment'></div>时不与兮吾谁尤，白鹤归兮河之洲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312379_comment'></div>苏台杳兮云正愁，唳华表兮天知否。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1312379_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年4月</a>　方岳为狼山寺僧恭率翁作《狼山寺重建僧堂记》。集中有致恭衰翁诗文多篇。<div id='poem_1312331' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312331' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312331?labeling=true' target='_blank'>狼山寺重建僧堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312331")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312331_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312331'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312331'>狼山面江腋海，以山水之胜望淮南，而寺又最古，异时户外之屦常满，钟鱼铿鍧出云雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312331_comment'></div>独所谓僧堂者久不葺，绳枢縻栋，惧将压焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312331_comment'></div>率翁居无几何，彻而新之，向之靳不捐一金者欢施惟恐后，积至三千万，不日月而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312331_comment'></div>百楹相扶，有严有翼，而明楼闳丽轩豁，殆与此山相雄长，盖今之所有而昔之所无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312331_comment'></div>余闻学道者岩栖而谷处，巢跧而雪立，其木石之与居，鹿豕之与游，虽把茅盖头，犹以为泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312331_comment'></div>乃今荫华屋，连高甍，有五侯邸第，溟涬然弟之者，不趺而坐，不胁而卧，其亦有所思乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312331_comment'></div>海山茫茫，江月洸洸，率翁试尝以余言问之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312331_comment'></div>翁名慧恭，字敬可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312331_comment'></div>是役也，始于端平三年十二月之戊子，成于明年嘉熙正月之己巳，而记于是年四月之壬午云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1312331_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　七月，元蒙军自光州、信阳抵合肥。十二月，赵葵于前线奏捷。《小稿诗集》卷二二有《十二月二十四日雪盖予三年于淮终见此耳时东师援淝捷书西来走笔呈赵公借宫奴与幕友一醉》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　除日，方岳作《除日雪甚约客不至乃拥貂骤马于郊外独饮摘星楼举鞭谢客曰未可使城中诸公知之但当夸与灞桥驴子上郑五耳》<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：方岳居赵幕期间，爱国诗词颇多，思旨深远，词气豪迈，乃其前期竭力主战思想的集中体现。）</span><div id='poem_64540' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64540' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/64540?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除日雪甚约客不至乃拥貂骤马于郊外独饮摘星楼举鞭谢客曰未可使城中诸公知之但当誇与灞桥驴子上郑五耳</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_64540")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_64540_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_64540'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_64540'>扬州二十四桥月，莫作灞桥同调看。<div id='poem_sentence_0_64540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_64540'>诗果位登银色界，酒风流倚玉阑干。<div id='poem_sentence_1_64540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64540'>六花比似琼花巧，一岁翻成两岁寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_64540'>明日屠苏催短鬓，过从更觉欠袁安。<div id='poem_sentence_3_64540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_64540'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_64540_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　高定子迁太府少卿，升计度转运副使，方岳作《贺高运使》<div id='poem_1311777' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311777' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311777?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺高运使启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311777")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311777_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311777'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311777'>伏审辍自鹓墀，诞分虎节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311777_comment'></div>引星辰于碧海，有开蜀道之天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311777_comment'></div>将礼乐之皇华，不远长安之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311777_comment'></div>窃窥帝意，深有庙谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311777_comment'></div>若曰当宁，思古名臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311777_comment'></div>其维武侯，为时王佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311777_comment'></div>每读《出师》之表，无惭《伊训》之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311777_comment'></div>虽吴魏自裂而三分，岂汉贼可岐而两立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311777_comment'></div>草庐所蕴，竹简莫传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311777_comment'></div>盖卧龙之蛰匪徒然，繄流马之运其小者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311777_comment'></div>乃眷西土而凛有遗迹，宽予北顾者讵无若人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311777_comment'></div>幸今天道之好还，大快人情之共愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311777_comment'></div>何止扼亢而拊其背，已焚老上之庭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311777_comment'></div>尽皆践土而食其毛，载沐汉家之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311777_comment'></div>然一方之初靖，又强敌之可忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311777_comment'></div>试以《唐书》与《五代史》而考之，其见于中国亦三百年而馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311777_comment'></div>既吞噬之无厌，终蚕食之堪虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311777_comment'></div>如使争雄于封域之间，奚啻鼾睡于卧榻之侧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311777_comment'></div>吾恐患方深耳，见谓一秦之复生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1311777_comment'></div>公其起而图之，纵无百参而何缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1311777_comment'></div>若然则朝家之委寄，夫岂惟使者之将输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1311777_comment'></div>闻之缙绅，伟哉纶綍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1311777_comment'></div>恭惟道山蓬莱之胸次，楚泽云梦之笔端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1311777_comment'></div>当其排阊阖而呈琅玕，信已跨昆崙而餐沆瀣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1311777_comment'></div>乃烦视草，出以飞刍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1311777_comment'></div>意者复周土宇而兴六月之师，其必章汉天声而决千里之胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1311777_comment'></div>饱吾貔虎，靖彼烟尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1311777_comment'></div>儆军实而申之，不留敌以遗君父；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1311777_comment'></div>无只轮之返者，迄安边而立功名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1311777_comment'></div>使鼎湖弓剑之藏，与渭上衣冠之庙，王气开而天地辟，远氛扫而河洛清，则多多益办之勋，皆陈陈相因之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1311777_comment'></div>以故诵言乎诸葛，不复比数于萧何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1311777_comment'></div>某布所闻，匪为之佞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1311777_comment'></div>逢此盛举，未尝不叹曰江左之有夷吾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1311777_comment'></div>迟之几何，将亦相戒以中国之相司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1311777_comment'></div>惟抵掌而谈天下之事，敢折腰而及吾身之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1311777_comment'></div>其若翘瞻，莫殚忻颂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1311777_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　袁甫迁中书舍人，转将作监。《小稿》卷一三《贺袁大监》，均有贺袁甫者。嘉熙三年，袁甫权兵部尚书，暂兼吏部尚书，致函于方岳，岳作《回袁吏部》<span class='inlineComment2'>（袁甫，字广征，鄞人，理学家袁燮之子，嘉定十六年知徽州，与方岳有书。）</span><div id='poem_1312051' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312051' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312051?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回袁吏部劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1237年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312051")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312051_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312051'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312051'>某维日史君之庐山而东也，秋风撤棘，为地主者方陪主司诸公，重客在门，礼多违者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312051_comment'></div>江皋一别，鸿宿之春蔼如，贺上签房今犹未能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312051_comment'></div>不图狼画翩翩，挟蕲竹之霜而至矣，感何可言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312051_comment'></div>太微二十五星，岂久为沙上留者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312051_comment'></div>会且归矣，仪我玉斑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312051_comment'></div>思皇召纶，日月以冀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1312051_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　在扬州，进礼兵部架阁，添差淮东制司干官。是年，国事家事，多有封岳仕途和思想影响颇大者：其一，开始与赵葵不和。其二，因力反议和而忤参知政事史嵩之。其三，父钦祖病笃，兄病殁，岳欲携父返故里。作品：《水调歌头·九日多景楼用吴侍郎（户部）韵》、《贺新郎·别吴侍郎》<div id='poem_65049' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_65049' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/65049?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>九日多景楼用吴侍郎韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_65049")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_65049_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_65049'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_65049'>醉我一壶玉，了此十分秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_65049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_65049'>江涛还此，当日击楫渡中流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_65049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_65049'>问讯重阳烟雨，俯仰人间今古，此意渺沧洲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_65049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_65049'>天地几今夕，举白与君浮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_65049_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_65049'>旧黄花，新白发，笑重游。<div id='poem_sentence_4_65049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_65049'>满船明月犹在，何日<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_65049", 65049, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>大刀头</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_65049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_65049'>谁跨扬州鹤去，已怨故山猿老，借箸欲前筹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_65049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_65049'>莫倚阑干北，天际是神州。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_65049_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_65087' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_65087' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/65087?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新郎 别吴侍郎吴时闲居，数夕前梦枯梅成<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>林，一枝独秀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_65087")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_65087_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_65087'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_65087'>霜月寒如洗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_65087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_65087'>问梅花、经年何事，尚迷烟水。<div id='poem_sentence_1_65087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_65087'>梦著翠霞寻好句，新雪阑干独倚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_65087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_65087'>见竹外、一枝横蕊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_65087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_65087'>已占百花头上了，料诗情、不但江山耳。<div id='poem_sentence_4_65087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_65087'>春已逗，有佳思。<div id='poem_sentence_5_65087_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_65087'>一香吹动人间世。<div id='poem_sentence_6_65087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_65087'>奈何地、丛篁低碧，巧相亏蔽。<div id='poem_sentence_7_65087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_65087'>尽让春风凡草木，便做云根石底。<div id='poem_sentence_8_65087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_65087'>但留取、微酸滋味。<div id='poem_sentence_9_65087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_65087'>除却林逋无人识，算岁寒、只是天知己。<div id='poem_sentence_10_65087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_65087'>休弄玉，怨迟暮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_65087_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年5月</a>　李宗勉自签枢院事作参知政事，岳有《贺李签枢》、《贺李参政》<div id='poem_1311781' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311781' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311781?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺李佥枢启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311781")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311781_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311781'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311781'>恭审望尊书殿，位峻机庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311781_comment'></div>惟吉士劢相我国家，师言允穆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311781_comment'></div>用真儒无敌于天下，疆事敉宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311781_comment'></div>于赫圣谟，有嘉王佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311781_comment'></div>恭惟以二典之书鸣治世，以三馆之学仪清朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311781_comment'></div>非尧舜不陈于前，大吾君之无过；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311781_comment'></div>将文武未坠于地，幸斯道之有传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311781_comment'></div>仁义一言，明良千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311781_comment'></div>式庆风云之会，聿临枢斗之躔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311781_comment'></div>遭时多难，属望尤切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311781_comment'></div>繄天下一家罔不率，其孰使然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311781_comment'></div>今左右国人皆曰贤，必能办此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311781_comment'></div>曾何患乎烟尘，当自靖夫疆土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311781_comment'></div>盖天开奠枕之期，维日望止戈之武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311781_comment'></div>言观伟绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311781_comment'></div>敬伫褒纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311781_comment'></div>军旅俎豆之事尝闻之，正有关于轻重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311781_comment'></div>太尉丞相之尊则等耳，行兼佩于安危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311781_comment'></div>某传诵制函，钧陶化冶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1311781_comment'></div>命将帅以卫国，誓殚折箠之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1311781_comment'></div>修政事以宁边，倾听借筹之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1311781_comment'></div>具瞻岩石，用济巨川。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1311781_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1311780' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311780' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311780?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺李参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311780")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311780_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311780'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311780'>恭审诞扬制册，参柄政机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311780_comment'></div>当圣贤驰骛之时，聿思元老；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311780_comment'></div>觊道德安强之效，迄底丕平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311780_comment'></div>简在帝心，于皇庙论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311780_comment'></div>恭惟养其气以刚大，尊所闻而高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311780_comment'></div>姚崇应变而宋璟守文，兼负经纶之蕴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311780_comment'></div>玄龄善谋而如晦能断，克成综核之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311780_comment'></div>自缵武于枢庭，茂结知于宸极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311780_comment'></div>明良千载，仁义一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311780_comment'></div>伊欲天下皆尧舜之民，正以胸中有孔周之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311780_comment'></div>会羽檄适忧于丙枕，宜锋车趣驾于庚牌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311780_comment'></div>王曰归哉，旧弼为中朝之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311780_comment'></div>天其或者，太平当今日之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311780_comment'></div>遄观介圭，入陪台衮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311780_comment'></div>共徯巨川之济，式隆岩石之瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311780_comment'></div>泰阶同符，间两社以为公辅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311780_comment'></div>神鼎增重，有一德以享天心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311780_comment'></div>倾听白麻，登延黄阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311780_comment'></div>某亲逢盛事，思见熙辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1311780_comment'></div>甲兵之问不至庙堂，盖边臣之至愿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1311780_comment'></div>忠信之行匪徒州里，惟公相之所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1311780_comment'></div>嘉与函生，悉归陶冶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1311780_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1311780_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　杜杲守庐州有战功，诏以安抚庐州，进太府卿、淮西制置副使兼转运使。岳为赵葵拟《代贺杜安抚》、《代贺杜制置》<span class='inlineComment2'>（杜杲，字子昕，邵武人，兼文武才，累迁工部、刑部、吏部尚书。岳有酬和《祭杜尚书》文。）</span><div id='poem_1311788' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311788' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311788?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代贺杜安抚启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311788")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311788_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311788'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311788'>伏审涣发纶函，晋登藩岳，勋业聿高于淝水，声威诞播于淮壖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311788_comment'></div>恭惟国之荩臣，今之儒帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311788_comment'></div>崇诗书，说礼乐，窥圣域之妙而探其心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311788_comment'></div>安边境，立功名，关武夫之口而夺之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311788_comment'></div>此所谓有用之学，赖以济多难之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311788_comment'></div>故虽干戈之屡侵，顿惊风鹤而宵遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311788_comment'></div>肆攽一札，增重十连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311788_comment'></div>帝曰愈哉，有夷吾而何患；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311788_comment'></div>功亦伟矣，召季布而可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311788_comment'></div>某闻命云初，愬风以喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311788_comment'></div>两淮犹左右手，正资运掉之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311788_comment'></div>九重披舆地图，更伫经纶之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311788_comment'></div>敢因庆幅，𣶂赞壮猷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1311788_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1311794' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311794' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311794?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代贺杜制置启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311794")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311794_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311794'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311794'>伏审进班司府，分梱藩垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311794_comment'></div>谢玄成淝水之勋，彼师其遁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311794_comment'></div>裴度任淮西之寄，我武维皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311794_comment'></div>谅草木之皆兵，徯关河之入贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311794_comment'></div>恭惟以少陵之诗名而自比于稷契，以阿房之赋手而高论于唐虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311794_comment'></div>精神之折遐冲，不愆于素；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311794_comment'></div>谋虑之憺勍敌，克壮其猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311794_comment'></div>故能全孤城于百战之馀，于此见真儒为万人之杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311794_comment'></div>既勒铭于丹地，乃授钺于青冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311794_comment'></div>顾惟风尘澒洞之秋，要有意气激昂之暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311794_comment'></div>平居推赤心而置人腹，其孰不怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311794_comment'></div>缓急蹈白刃则得士情，何战弗克！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311794_comment'></div>矧天意之歼敌，适岁星之照吴，国岂赖盟，兵毋撤警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311794_comment'></div>惟事事备乃其无患，愿修军旅之定规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311794_comment'></div>言人人殊则罔成功，更极宾僚之高选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311794_comment'></div>聿观伟业，丕对殊褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311794_comment'></div>某密迩邻光，驩传帝赉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311794_comment'></div>闑以内闑以外，喜尽寄于爪牙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311794_comment'></div>陕以东陕以西，赖相依于唇齿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1311794_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
临安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bd90fa1d739d4399881e71dc44d0f533_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bd90fa1d739d4399881e71dc44d0f533");'><span id='bd90fa1d739d4399881e71dc44d0f533_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1242')">1241-1242年</a>，44-45岁</div><div id='bd90fa1d739d4399881e71dc44d0f533' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1241')">1241年</a>　丁父忧，服阙，秋离家赴临安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1242&endYear=1242')">1242年</a>　起为刑工部架阁，居官五十六日，罢职闲居。作品：《最高楼·壬寅生日》<div id='poem_65096' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_65096' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/65096?labeling=true' target='_blank'>最高楼<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>壬寅生日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1242年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_65096")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_65096_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_65096'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_65096'>溪南北，本自一渔舟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_65096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_65096'>烟雨几盟鸥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_65096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_65096'>白鱼不负鸬鹚杓，青蓑不减鹔鹴裘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_65096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_65096'>怎无端，贪射策，觅封侯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_65096_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_65096'>既不似、古人能识字。<div id='poem_sentence_4_65096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_65096'>又不似、今人能识事。<div id='poem_sentence_5_65096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_65096'>空老去，自宜休。<div id='poem_sentence_6_65096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_65096'>帝乡五十六朝暮，人间四十四春秋。<div id='poem_sentence_7_65096_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_65096'>问何如，茅一把，橘千头。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_65096_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1242&endYear=1242')">1242年2月</a>　赵葵赐进士出身，同知枢密院事，方岳为之拟《辞勉枢密使（二表）》<div id='poem_1311609' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311609' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311609?labeling=true' target='_blank'>督视辞免枢密使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1242年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311609")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311609_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311609'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311609'>边圉绎骚，敢惮师干之役；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311609_comment'></div>枢庭宥密，难叨使范之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311609_comment'></div>用荐沥于愚衷，觊终回于聪听<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311609_comment'></div>伏念臣屡更烦使，曾蔑微劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311609_comment'></div>维有之是以似之，窃愧西平之子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311609_comment'></div>今老矣无能为矣，盍投南岳之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311609_comment'></div>封章凡几上而乞骸，时事每一思而掩涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311609_comment'></div>适此交驰于羽檄，讵容高卧于岩廊！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311609_comment'></div>矧帷幄之无筹，孰执其咎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311609_comment'></div>既甲兵之有问，当诿之谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311609_comment'></div>将慷慨以请行，肯趑趄而避事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311609_comment'></div>惟是仍政涂之机柄，陟使领于神枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311609_comment'></div>过窃宠荣，实踰涯分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311609_comment'></div>恐匪在师之吉，有乖授任之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311609_comment'></div>伏望皇帝穆然周思，赫以独断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311609_comment'></div>念四郊多垒，非人臣媒利禄之时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311609_comment'></div>使五大在边，岂圣主驭英雄之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311609_comment'></div>无嫌反汗，俾遂牢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311609_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1311609_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1242&endYear=1242')">1242年2月</a>　为徽州守郑崇作《徽州平？仓记》<div id='poem_1312335' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312335' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312335?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽州平籴仓记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1242年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312335")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312335_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312335'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312335'>淳祐二年春，太守郑侯劝农于郊，有荷蓧而歌者曰：「田彼南山，维石龉龉，言刈我黍，不盈其筥」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312335_comment'></div>既又歌曰：「籴而珠乎，其曷春吾襦乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312335_comment'></div>炊而玉乎，其曷果吾腹乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312335_comment'></div>侯式车而听之，喟然叹曰：「噫，是力穑而啬收，有年而贵籴者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312335_comment'></div>徽民凿山而田，高耕入云者十半，其力贫而食贵，吾念之甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312335_comment'></div>独郡挻于火，民庐官寺，百役具兴，今幸复故初而力且匮，而吾且去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312335_comment'></div>虽然，吾渠以其匮、渠以其去而恝吾民哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312335_comment'></div>于是游观之娱、厨传之饰、岁时交邻之聘，苦积酌损，得十万缗，揭以为平籴本，俾有司秋入而春出之，以相循于无穷，氓也其何幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312335_comment'></div>虽然，知及在初，仁守在后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312335_comment'></div>使耿寿昌而在，常平法通百世无弊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312335_comment'></div>伐石以属之后子云，氓也抑何幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312335_comment'></div>虽然，涸辙之升斗，孰与相忘于江湖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312335_comment'></div>夏畦之桔槔，孰与无德于雨露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312335_comment'></div>侯归而报政，推此类为上具言之，氓也重何幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312335_comment'></div>侯名崇，字谦仲，吴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312335_comment'></div>是岁二月既望，郡人方某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1312335_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_1312291_comment'></div>风雨凄凄，鸡鸣喈喈，鹤山以之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312291_comment'></div>他山有石，可以攻玉，周卿以之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312291_comment'></div>淳祐二三十九，歙人方某书于桐庐舟中。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1312291_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1242&endYear=1242')">1242年4月</a>　史宾之知徽州府到官，方岳有《送史子贯归觐且迎妇也》诗。<div id='poem_64507' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64507' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_64507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64507'>尽有好山容对榻，却因吾子转思家。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
