ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1245&endYear=1245')">1245年</a>　在临安。任礼兵部架阁，寻除太学正兼景县府教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1245&endYear=1245')">1245年</a>　在临安，先后为左相范钟拟《赐衣带谢表》、《赐衣带鞍马谢表》等。<div id='poem_1311626' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311626' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311626?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐衣带谢表<span class='inlineComment2'>（以下代范丞相）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1245年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311626")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311626_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311626'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311626'>恩言狎至，聿高鸣玉之班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311626_comment'></div>命服斯皇，更佩环金之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311626_comment'></div>有华枯朽，难称荣光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311626_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>伏念臣家本绨袍，起从韦带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311626_comment'></div>半生贫苦，谁怜身世之寒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311626_comment'></div>一念艰虞，久觉腰围之减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311626_comment'></div>分归寻于短褐，何堪系于精镠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311626_comment'></div>敢意微躯，荐叨误渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311626_comment'></div>此盖恭遇皇帝，仁足以衣被四海，明足以约束群才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311626_comment'></div>文帝亲御弋绨，盛德蔑加于恭俭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311626_comment'></div>光皇自解佩绶，茂恩不替于贤劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311626_comment'></div>乃锡身章，于昭眷赉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311626_comment'></div>臣敢不书绅图报，束衽怀惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311626_comment'></div>又改为兮，不叹无衣之七；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311626_comment'></div>亦足敬也，庶逃终褫之三。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1311626_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1311627' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311627' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311627?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐衣带鞍马谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1245年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311627")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311627_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311627'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311627'>袭衣宝带，有腼梁鹈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311627_comment'></div>鞗革锡镠，更分厩驷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311627_comment'></div>于粲服乘之贲，何知俯偻之蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311627_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣寒故念于绨袍，驽不堪于羁勒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311627_comment'></div>矍铄哉是翁也，老矣奚为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311627_comment'></div>逢掖者儒服与，萧然何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311627_comment'></div>每念牛衣之泣卧，居惭马革之裹归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311627_comment'></div>敢意宠光，荣此衰朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311627_comment'></div>此盖恭遇皇帝，藩饰百度，鞭笞四陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311627_comment'></div>武王之一戎衣，将辑宁于华夏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311627_comment'></div>文帝之千里马，必驾驭于英雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311627_comment'></div>顾惟何人，亦攽异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311627_comment'></div>臣敢不曳娄图报，奔走服劳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311627_comment'></div>要之襋之，好人服之，第乏弥缝之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311627_comment'></div>瘏矣痡矣，云何吁矣，恐贻负乘之讥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1311627_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1245&endYear=1245')">1245年12月</a>　在临安，赵葵兼知两府，代之拟《除枢密使兼参知政事督视军马谢表》、《第二表》（见《小稿》卷一）<div id='poem_1311612' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311612' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311612?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除枢密使兼知政事督视军马谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1245年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311612")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311612_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311612'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311612'>假钺而督诸军，曾微威望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311612_comment'></div>进班而联二府，有腼恩徽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311612_comment'></div>制书不许于辞难，事任凛如于履薄<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311612_comment'></div>臣闻自昔艰难之会，聿求经济之材，使尽护于戎昭，用借筹于庙胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311612_comment'></div>故能出入将相，注意安危，内外修攘，兼资文武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311612_comment'></div>学力则有若臣浚之刚大，智名则有若臣鼎之高明，必惟斯人，始称上意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311612_comment'></div>如臣者器不足以适时用，识不足以烛事机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311612_comment'></div>仲淹胸中之百万兵，何能为役？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311612_comment'></div>富弼河朔之十三策，多见谓愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311612_comment'></div>徒以父教之忠，仰累圣知之误，遂跻两地，倏粤再期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311612_comment'></div>适军书飞羽之秋，敢安驽劣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311612_comment'></div>顾幕府重帅之任，曷称鹰扬！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311612_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝，旋转乾坤，辑宁海宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311612_comment'></div>非贤罔乂，谨一日万几之微；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311612_comment'></div>无竞维人，斡三军五兵之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311612_comment'></div>肆令愚陋，张我皇威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311612_comment'></div>臣敢不遵奉明谟，布昭圣武？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311612_comment'></div>惟当鞠躬而后已，其责在臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311612_comment'></div>若夫成功则不知，惟天祚宋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1311612_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1245&endYear=1245')">1245年12月</a>　在临安。嗣荣王与芮加少保，方岳为之作《代景献哋谢夫人号》、《代景献邸贺冬至》等。<div id='poem_1311642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311642?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代景献邸夫人封号谢表<span class='inlineComment2'>（时为讲官）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1245年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311642")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311642_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311642'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311642'>王假有家，展亲公族；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311642_comment'></div>妇无公事，进号小君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311642_comment'></div>与宗社以同休，等乾坤而莫报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311642_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>恭惟皇帝俭勤如禹，笃睦如尧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311642_comment'></div>八柄以驭臣工，聿先风化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311642_comment'></div>三纲以明夫妇，盖厚人伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311642_comment'></div>施及闺门，叨承爵邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311642_comment'></div>臣永肩伉俪，共载穹隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311642_comment'></div>诸侯曰夫人，愿已踰于有室；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311642_comment'></div>一德尊天子，怀永矢于维城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311642_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1311642_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1311644' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311644' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311644?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代景献邸冬至贺表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1245年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311644")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311644_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311644'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311644'>律回天统，阊阖日长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311644_comment'></div>春丽帝居，觚棱云暖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311644_comment'></div>于穆太和之世，有开刚长之期<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311644_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝天德出宁，人时敬授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311644_comment'></div>用众君子，伟阴霾之划开；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311644_comment'></div>更一化元，喜阳明之休复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311644_comment'></div>朋来七日，有仆万年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311644_comment'></div>臣猥奉宗藩，获瞻宸扆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311644_comment'></div>百兽率舞，亲逢皇帝推筴之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311644_comment'></div>六龙时乘，请祝国家过历之祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311644_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1311644_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1245&endYear=1245')">1245年</a>　在临安。作《答韩寺丞》、《送寺丞韩君守新安》<div id='poem_64511' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64511' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/64511?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送寺丞韩君守新安<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1245年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_64511")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_64511_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_64511'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_64511'>君家集有陆参序，老笔誇张歙大州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_64511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_64511'>三百年来非昔比，二千石喜得今侯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_64511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64511'>早田已槁曾关念，旧石虽奇不到收。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_64511'>沃沃桑麻山雨外，归欤氓亦买羸牛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_64511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_64511'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_64511_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_64510' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64510' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/64510?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1245年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_64510_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_64510'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_64510'>吾州可但佳山水，薰沐诗书自不同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_64510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_64510'>牧守曾留今相国，郡人况有我文公。<div id='poem_sentence_1_64510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64510'>诸贤雅欲相俎豆，一念底须多缿筒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_64510'>三十六峰吟更笔，只将无事过年丰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_64510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_64510'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_64510_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年</a>　在临安，由太学正迁宗学博士。作品：《轮封第二札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《小稿》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年2月</a>　范钟乞归，诏提举洞霄宫，任便居住。方岳先后为之拟《辞免左丞相表》及《谢表》、《辞免提举国史会要玉牒要略》、《辞免进书银绢》（附第二奏）、《辞免生日牲饩》、《辞免除职予祠侍读奏》（附第三奏）及《谢表》等等。<div id='poem_1311630' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311630' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311630?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免提举国史会要玉牒要略</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311630")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311630_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311630'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311630'>赞化均陶，一无可取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311630_comment'></div>提纲笔削，四者难并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311630_comment'></div>方此恳辞，讵容忝冒！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311630_comment'></div>伏念臣怀铅抱椠，本起诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311630_comment'></div>当轴秉钧，宁堪守相；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311630_comment'></div>自惭文墨，莫补汗青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311630_comment'></div>史有三长，与闻虽久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311630_comment'></div>虑无一得，典领何堪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311630_comment'></div>伏望圣慈毋循故常，趣还成涣，将令简册，罔愧诗书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1311630_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1311631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免进书银绢</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311631")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311631_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311631'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311631'>臣窃以提纲笔削，允谓故常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311631_comment'></div>出綍匪颁，曾微功实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311631_comment'></div>矧经一览，已锡茂恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311631_comment'></div>九式币馀，讵容滥予；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311631_comment'></div>百僚衮缺，何以具瞻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311631_comment'></div>欲节费浮，愿从臣始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311631_comment'></div>所有。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1311631_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1311633' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311633' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311633?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免生日牲饩</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311633")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311633_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311633'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311633'>臣切以后月之三日，实惟老臣之贱生，若稽故常，厥有礼赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311633_comment'></div>豫深兢惧，莫敢遑宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311633_comment'></div>盖以臣待罪宰庭，股肱无补，积愆私室，手足方亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311633_comment'></div>其间又虑春哨之或驰，上累宵忧之未艾，是殆家国多艰之日，殊非君臣相乐之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311633_comment'></div>所有臣生日牲饩等赐，欲望矜俞，亟从寝免。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1311633_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1311636' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311636' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311636?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除职予祠侍读奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311636")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311636_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311636'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311636'>臣猥以衰残之年，迫于危笃之疾，恳求骸骨，备沥肺肝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311636_comment'></div>方幸天意哀怜，奎章开允，恩隆眷厚，感极涕零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311636_comment'></div>而臣犹有区区之愚，不胜缕缕之渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311636_comment'></div>切以臣禀赋迂拙，遭逢圣明，久污清朝，遂跻元宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311636_comment'></div>顾微臣之谨畏，惟陛下之简知，外此无长，自量甚审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311636_comment'></div>既遂山林之衰老，已为天地之生成，而乃峻以文阶，冠于书殿，优游真馆，密勿经帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311636_comment'></div>凡往前归老之大臣，无今日便蕃之异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311636_comment'></div>人将不恕，臣亦何颜！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311636_comment'></div>伏望圣慈尽免殊恩，曲矜晚节，但令閒退，即是宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311636_comment'></div>所有特转两官、除观文殿大学士、醴泉观使兼侍读恩命，臣不敢祗受外，欲乞别降指挥，许归田里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311636_comment'></div>臣不胜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1311636_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年4月</a>　丘岳兼两淮屯田副使，方岳与之相知较早，谊甚笃厚。《小稿》卷十有《回丘运使》、《与丘运使丘》时丘在淮东，主漕运。<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《小稿》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_1311723' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311723' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311723?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回丘运使冬书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311723")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311723_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311723'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311723'>绣壁春融，有永汉宫之日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311723_comment'></div>缇函晓袭，聿飞郇翰之云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311723_comment'></div>佩雅意之相宣，愧颂言之已后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311723_comment'></div>此盖某官文成唾玉，谊重断金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311723_comment'></div>惠我双鲤鱼，共喜甘芬之错落；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311723_comment'></div>出呼五花马，第惊节物之峥嵘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311723_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1311723_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1311724' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311724' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311724?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与丘运使冬书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311724")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311724_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311724'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311724'>玉筦春回，已动扬州之梅兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311724_comment'></div>霜台云煖，遄飞词掖之芝香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311724_comment'></div>若时繁釐，集我儒彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311724_comment'></div>某官苍璧之粹秀，黄钟之函和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311724_comment'></div>消群慝于六阴，慨有澄清之略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311724_comment'></div>复亨期于七日，徯陈平治之谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311724_comment'></div>式对迎长，于皇入觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311724_comment'></div>某闻欢声之旁午，嘉幸会于同寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311724_comment'></div>赠我明月珠，敬佩书绅之感；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311724_comment'></div>报之青玉案，敢忘献袜之铭！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311724_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1311724_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年8月</a>　赐刘克庄进士出身，时年六十。周密五十岁。王焘知祁门县事。《小稿》卷七有《通王宰》，《小稿》卷二《宗学进墨碑》（自注：时为宗博）；《御书太学及崇化堂武学及立武学堂牌谢表》（自注：时为宗博）。作《祭杜丞相（范）》、《祭徐侍郎（元杰）》、《徐二卿（元杰）与彭监帖》、《程少章文稿（序）》等。应海门方处义请为其守视父墓之庐作《致存堂铭》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年</a>　黟人奚从青（字朝瑞）来访，方岳有《回奚监酒》、《回奚朝瑞》等。<span class='inlineComment2'>（奚氏工诗，景定六年进士及第，官祠部员外郎。）</span><div id='poem_1311833' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311833' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311833?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回奚监酒启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311833")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311833_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311833'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311833'>粤起鳣堂，小留虎帐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311833_comment'></div>谈笑青油幕，安用腐儒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311833_comment'></div>飞堕碧云笺，甚惭乡友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311833_comment'></div>此岂醉翁之误我，政恐空山之怨人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311833_comment'></div>不曰师乎，何厌广文之冷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311833_comment'></div>拔其尤者，孰云处士之良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311833_comment'></div>尚邀枌社之春，毋靳药言之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311833_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1311833_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312055' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312055' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312055?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回奚朝瑞劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312055")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312055_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312055'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312055'>某当岁除穷忙，忽奉墨妙，首之以邦君诸侯之礼貌，申之以诸老先生之题品，二陆入洛，宁复过此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312055_comment'></div>朝瑞一日声名霸吾州矣，泥涂曳尾，惟有健羡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312055_comment'></div>独所谓舌本澜翻者得于夜观一语，此某之所缩颈掩耳而疾走者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312055_comment'></div>某虽无识，岂敢误人以澜翻者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312055_comment'></div>士之垂世，恐自别有所立，不在文字，况后世之诗、文字之靡乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312055_comment'></div>欧阳子称尹师鲁之文「简而有法」，其家子弟请益，子曰：「简而有法惟《春秋》足以当之，某于师鲁不薄矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312055_comment'></div>不图今者朝瑞亦云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312055_comment'></div>严子陵谓侯霸之史曰，卖菜乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312055_comment'></div>求多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312055_comment'></div>敢以是箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312055_comment'></div>某学不足以窥朝瑞之藩，援引非据，简而有法，出诗几头地，博达如朝瑞，当自知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312055_comment'></div>某之此言其为自谋，信有罪矣，其为朝瑞谋也忠，不识能受之否乎？</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1312055_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年</a>　在临安，除秘书郎，后赴建康，充赵葵幕参议官。寻差知南康军。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1b5f78387eef44058ff634b0b56ccecb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1b5f78387eef44058ff634b0b56ccecb");'><span id='1b5f78387eef44058ff634b0b56ccecb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=-100000&endYear=1262')">1262年</a>，65岁</div><div id='1b5f78387eef44058ff634b0b56ccecb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1260&endYear=1260')">1260年</a>　居家。方岳万年，方回来访，失甲子，待考。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1261&endYear=1261')">1261年</a>　在家闲居。十月，程元凤授特进，观文殿大学士，醴泉观使兼侍读，有《讷齐集》。方岳有《题讷齐》诗，疑作于此年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1262')">1262年</a>　卒于家，葬荷花坞。有《秋崖小稿》行于世，重修《南北史》一百一十卷。《宗维训录》十卷，未传。<br />年份未详　是年，刘辰翁举进士，以廷试封策忤贾似道，列丙等。王寔知祁门县事，方岳作《答王宰》<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
邵武
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9baa3a762b4b41739f4885529c0eb17e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9baa3a762b4b41739f4885529c0eb17e");'><span id='9baa3a762b4b41739f4885529c0eb17e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年</a>，53岁</div><div id='9baa3a762b4b41739f4885529c0eb17e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年夏</a>　“未至邵武二百里，峒顽作，驰急足榜谕之。寇 知威名，迎拜车下而散。”（《洪传》），方岳为此作《谢放罪表（邵武）》<span class='inlineComment2'>（由《小稿》卷二五《答李兄》知方岳于是年年初尚未赴任。《小稿诗集》卷一九《春雨庚戌》知，是年仲春，岳尚居家。《小稿诗集》卷二○《去年五月十七庐山祷而雨尝有诗今年五月十七邵武祷而晴因用韻》知方岳赴邵武，当在是年夏季。谢堂知徽州，六月到官。方岳《回乡郡谢守》之“六月到官”与前“五月十七”祷晴不相符，疑《徽志》误。）</span><div id='poem_1311621' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311621' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311621?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢放罪表<span class='inlineComment2'>（邵武）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1250年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311621")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311621_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311621'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311621'>挺刃胥戕，刑兹无赦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311621_comment'></div>抗章自劾，罪在专诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311621_comment'></div>恩言沛若于江河，法令昭如于星日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311621_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>伏以此邦之俗，佩犊带牛，轻生之民，喜人怒兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311621_comment'></div>而属者常行之狱讼，乃率然擅动于干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311621_comment'></div>鸡犬为空，使二人身首之异处；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311621_comment'></div>猿狙皆怒，宜一时血气之愤张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311621_comment'></div>臣方此来，亟其驰入，惟恐变成于瞬息，幸而令信于嚚顽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311621_comment'></div>乃正邦刑，以纾众怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311621_comment'></div>虽杀人者死，汉网恢恢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311621_comment'></div>然大德曰生，尧仁荡荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311621_comment'></div>敢不请而论诀，亦何意于矜容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311621_comment'></div>慈盖恭遇皇帝，惟德动天，以义制事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311621_comment'></div>念郡纲泯泯，追胥何以兵为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311621_comment'></div>谓祖训明明，犯法惟有剑耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311621_comment'></div>用布亏除之令，尽捐专辄之辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311621_comment'></div>臣继今以思，若古有训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311621_comment'></div>断者不可复属，凛如上帝之监临；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311621_comment'></div>杀之宁失不经，敢负本朝之仁厚？</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1311621_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='5419fc6df2e94e45972b128a08648d3f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5419fc6df2e94e45972b128a08648d3f");'><span id='5419fc6df2e94e45972b128a08648d3f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1253')">1250-1253年</a>，53-56岁</div><div id='5419fc6df2e94e45972b128a08648d3f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年</a>　知邵武军，作《邵武军到任谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《小稿》卷二，实为谢表，实皆抗言。佞臣贾似道实导致南宋覆灭之祸首。方岳能早识其奸，不畏强暴，挺身斥之，讼之庙堂；其刚直勇毅，浩然正气，亦诚可贵。）</span><div id='poem_1311646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311646?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邵武到任谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1250年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311646")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311646'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311646'>以柳易播，尚误宽恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311646_comment'></div>自江入闽，已祗远戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311646_comment'></div>感叹圣朝之仁厚，矜容臣子之赣愚<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311646_comment'></div>伏念臣守刚而乏沉潜，学朴而少涵养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311646_comment'></div>事人以直道，岂今世之能容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311646_comment'></div>得封如曲钩，亦平生之不取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311646_comment'></div>惟知公是，未觉昨非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311646_comment'></div>粤从督议之参商，出守庐山之僻小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311646_comment'></div>可以悔矣，郑商人之环何必争；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311646_comment'></div>抑有疑焉，齐楚侯之地不相及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1311646_comment'></div>夫奚湖广之饟所，具析江东之守臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1311646_comment'></div>不能忍于一惭，已自甘于三黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1311646_comment'></div>为臣惧者，皆曰南阳帝亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1311646_comment'></div>惟天知之，乃谓东朝公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1311646_comment'></div>第与更其竹使，亦不俟于瓜时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1311646_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇皇帝遍覆无私，容光必照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1311646_comment'></div>天下事惟其是而已，何间贱微？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1311646_comment'></div>我之心亦有曲者乎，一惟端直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1311646_comment'></div>故虽肺腑之请，曾靡毫釐之偏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1311646_comment'></div>肆令危踪，无失故步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1311646_comment'></div>臣敢不仰凭公溥，益劢直方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1311646_comment'></div>毋虐茕独而畏高明，安用前车之戒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1311646_comment'></div>与致平理而销愁叹，勉为后效之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1311646_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1311646_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1251&endYear=1251')">1251年</a>　在邵武。是年正月，兼右司郎官拜监察御史兼崇政殿说书程元凤上书斥左相郑清之久专国柄，老不任事，监察御史潘凯亦劾清之。方岳与潘凯交深，卷二七有《答潘南夫》。宝祐三年，潘凯任刑部侍郎，方岳有《与潘侍郎》，另有《潘君诗卷（序）》<div id='poem_1312081' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312081' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312081?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答潘南夫劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1251年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312081")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312081_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312081'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312081'>得所惠教，其意若有不能释然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312081_comment'></div>诸妄校尉已下材能不及中，往往以军功取封侯，飞将军顾独不得与为比，虽霸陵醉翁亦将不能释然于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312081_comment'></div>虽然，世所谓仕宦者优戏耳，适舆台之，骤衣冠之，政自不满饱老郭郎一笑，本来面目初无尔许事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312081_comment'></div>愿执事寘之碧玉之山、青罗之江，着我其间，要是不恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312081_comment'></div>同班序引，自是君家县令箴，所不如此言，将无面见北山猿鹤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312081_comment'></div>我日斯迈而月斯征，各相勉旃，毋负畴昔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1312081_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1251&endYear=1251')">1251年11月</a>　吴潜为右丞相，《小稿》卷二二有《与吴相公》，然此书未言乞惩廖姓事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年</a>　在邵武。春会返里，未几又回邵武。作《春盤》诗。<div id='poem_64930' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64930' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/64930?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春盘</a><span class='authorDate'>（壬子）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_64930")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_64930_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_64930'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_64930'>莱服根松缕冰玉，蒌蒿苗肥点寒绿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_64930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_64930'>霜鞭行茁软于酥，雪树生钉肥胜肉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_64930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64930'>与吾同味蔊丝辣，知我长贫韭菹熟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_64930'>更蒸豚压花层层，略糁凫成金粟粟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_64930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_64930'>青红饾饤映梅柳，紫翠招邀醉松竹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_64930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_64930'>擎将<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_64930", 64930, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>碧脆</span>捲月明，嚼出宫商带诗馥。<div id='poem_sentence_5_64930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_64930'>赐幡羞上老人头，家园不负将军腹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_64930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_64930'>人生行乐未渠央，物意趋新自相续。<div id='poem_sentence_7_64930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_64930'>五十三翁日落山，三百六旬车转毂。<div id='poem_sentence_8_64930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_64930'>不妨细雨看梅花，且喜春风到茅屋。<div id='poem_sentence_9_64930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_64930'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_64930_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年</a>　在邵武。春会返里，未几又回邵武。作《满江红·壬子生日》<div id='poem_65104' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_65104' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/65104?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红 壬子生日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1252年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_65104")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_65104_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_65104'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_65104'>晓傍苍崖，滴寒露、研朱点易。<div id='poem_sentence_0_65104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_65104'>五十四卦为归妹，惟幽人吉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_65104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_65104'>彼美人兮春上下，如吾徒者山南北。<div id='poem_sentence_2_65104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_65104'>辨一生、坚壁卧烟霞，诗无敌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_65104_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_65104'>人间世，胶中漆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_65104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_65104'>功名事，刀头蜜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_65104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_65104'>放乾坤醉眼，看朱成碧。<div id='poem_sentence_6_65104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_65104'>曾共梅花相尔汝，尽教雪后无消息。<div id='poem_sentence_7_65104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_65104'>莫怕寒、容易嫁东风，春狼藉。<div id='poem_sentence_8_65104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_65104'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_65104_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年</a>　在邵武。春会返里，未几又回邵武。作《跋师绍书华严经》文。<div id='poem_1312325' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312325' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312325?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋师绍书华严经</a><span class='authorDate'>（1252年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312325")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312325_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312325'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312325'>乃岁壬午，予学星于九龙山，识优婆塞，亡何得度，号曰智仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312325_comment'></div>别三十年，如一弹指，忽生亿念，不厌疲劳，自其山居，来诣予所，瞻仰作礼而白：予言仁者，我于别后，不敢懈怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312325_comment'></div>于我末法，妙饰庄严，堂殿斋庐，非复曩昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312325_comment'></div>有徒师绍，庵于高环，誓愿精勤，而作佛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312325_comment'></div>以大海墨，及须弥笔，积日累月，书《华严经》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312325_comment'></div>推仁垂慈，同一赞叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312325_comment'></div>予闻言已，生大欢喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312325_comment'></div>思昔大父，在家出家，尝书是经，作我镇宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312325_comment'></div>予嘉尔绍，慨念我祖，合爪西向，为说偈言：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1312325'>我闻昔有善知识，发大勇猛精进心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312325_comment'></div>欲书诸经了无有，但握爪为书空相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312325_comment'></div>其人既去其处存，虽无是经经不灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312325_comment'></div>天龙护持此处所，自然严净两不濡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312325_comment'></div>彼刹尘中所见闻，无不赞叹罕有事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312325_comment'></div>而一比丘独抚掌，乃言止是半藏经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312325_comment'></div>是知一切有为法，受想行识皆为累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312325_comment'></div>世主妙严及行愿，岂可色见声音求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312325_comment'></div>挥毫径入佛三妙，人人清净华严经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312325_comment'></div>我观经卷八十一，卷凡几品品几字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312325_comment'></div>一字一画一心具，心心修习尽未来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312325_comment'></div>于一毫端能放光，一一普现法界性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312325_comment'></div>稽首吾翁大长者，所成就非写经故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312325_comment'></div>为我问讯彼上人，云何了證真实际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312325_comment'></div>百一十城无可参，陶泓毛颖俱成佛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1312325_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1312325'>淳祐壬子七月下浣，居士方某见闻随喜，并此妄语，一忏悔之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1312325_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年3月</a>　三月，知徽州谢堂除工部郎中魏了翁子军器监丞魏克愚来守。《小稿》卷二四《回乡郡谢守》、《又答谢守》，均写于是年。<div id='poem_1312056' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312056' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312056?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回乡郡谢守劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1252年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312056")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312056_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312056'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312056'>某入山之深，入林之密，虽一裘一葛，安乐棠阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312056_comment'></div>龚黄之仁，罔间幽谷，惟日与芸夫荛子啸歌夕阳袯襫之间而莫之敢书者，屏废之人法当如是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312056_comment'></div>属有客谓某曰，史君方上政最进郎秩，子奚贺之后？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312056_comment'></div>某应之曰，史君将跻极品，踵相接也，奚贺之先！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312056_comment'></div>语犹未寒，缇骑来下，不图吾邦君之抚存其一介氓如此其厚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312056_comment'></div>慨思前载其弃置宽閒之野，流落寂寞之滨者，不为时所𨈆藉则亦幸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312056_comment'></div>至访问其穷独，慰劳其胼胝，所谓此事今无，古或闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312056_comment'></div>某敢不整其黄冠，拜手以谢！</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1312056_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312198' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312198' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312198?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又答谢守劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1252年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312198")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312198_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312198'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312198'>某仰惟皇上神毫之妙冠绝前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312198_comment'></div>平生妄想，以为万有一得侍清閒，敢拜稽手，乞「千崖秋气高」之诗以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312198_comment'></div>乃自绝于天，此念永已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312198_comment'></div>不图戏下分其有馀者以镇茅屋，乃又适是「秋气清」之句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312198_comment'></div>虽非上之所以亲赐小臣者，而云汉昭回，何往而非近天子之光也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312198_comment'></div>某九顿首以受赐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1312198_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　在邵武。冬，返故里。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年5月</a>　赐礼部进士姚勉以下及第、出身有差。程元凤从弟程元岳同榜及第，度宗时权工部侍郎，有《山窗集》。祁门人程鸣凤为武状元，《小稿》卷二二有《与程朝阳》<span class='inlineComment2'>（程鸣凤，字朝阳，和善人。文武兼备，累迁知德庆府（广东肇庆），有《读史发微》三十卷。）</span><div id='poem_1311996' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311996' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311996?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与程朝阳劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1253年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311996")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311996_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311996'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311996'>某自闻榜帖，为之喜不自持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311996_comment'></div>屏居山林，一字不入帝城，所谓此膝不屈于人若干年，今为公屈矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311996_comment'></div>伏惟大对昕庭，遂魁天下，不惟居家积累有此盛事，而成吾宅相，亦与光荣，先公有知，岂不含笑地下！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311996_comment'></div>夫是以不得不一书为贺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311996_comment'></div>中外兄弟不同它人徒贺而已焉者，古人有言，盛名之下难居，犹愿贤表留之意，此则不肖者区区持赠之心耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311996_comment'></div>时方袢暑，惟珍爱自厚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1311996_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　费翊知祁门县事，《小稿》卷三六有《答费宰》<div id='poem_64993' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64993' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/64993?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答费宰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1253年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_64993")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_64993_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_64993'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_64993'>野人拙生事，瓶粟盖无几。<div id='poem_sentence_0_64993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_64993'>唯有松下风，领略时一至。<div id='poem_sentence_1_64993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64993'>迩来风亦无，抱瓮岂得已。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_64993'>赖有大夫公，入山唤龙起。<div id='poem_sentence_3_64993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_64993'>铁笛横秋潭，山骨冰诗髓。<div id='poem_sentence_4_64993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_64993'>归来白云篇，出语更清驶。<div id='poem_sentence_5_64993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_64993'>自非境中人，其孰能与此。<div id='poem_sentence_6_64993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_64993'>吾等才哙伍，君才与丕倍。<div id='poem_sentence_7_64993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_64993'>一闻老农言，遽得言外意。<div id='poem_sentence_8_64993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_64993'>径烦写呈佛，十年亦中岁。<div id='poem_sentence_9_64993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_64993'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_64993_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　在邵武，暮春作《上巳溪泛》<div id='poem_64173' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64173' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/64173?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上巳溪汎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1253年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_64173")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_64173_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_64173'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_64173'>舴艋舟轻暖欲酣，鸬鹚杓重老何堪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_64173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_64173'>风霜两鬓五十五，杨柳几番三月三。<div id='poem_sentence_1_64173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64173'>禊帖又逢今癸丑，兰亭仍是旧东南。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_64173'>死生政亦寻常事，却笑诸贤苦未谙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_64173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_64173'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_64173_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　方岳与知州魏克愚过从甚密。集中《回魏监丞》计十篇。是年应邀为作《徽州重建庆礼桥记》<div id='poem_1312343' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312343' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312343?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽州重建庆丰桥记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1253年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312343")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312343_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312343'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312343'>宝祐改元，新安郡浮桥成，太守临邛魏侯克愚使其僚王宗说庀之，而使其民方岳记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312343_comment'></div>词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1312343'>自古在昔，胙邦建侯，四达其疆，庐积梁舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312343_comment'></div>有圮弗兴，是谓失政，君子即之，觇陈议郑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312343_comment'></div>匪川靡梁，不能为国，乃心匪民，则莫我恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312343_comment'></div>周官吕命，职在有司，民自为民，曾尔勿思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312343_comment'></div>宪宪魏侯，鹤山之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312343_comment'></div>鹤山之子，宁弗知此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312343_comment'></div>乃辟贡闱，乃增贡籍，政恬事熙，靡纤不葺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312343_comment'></div>乃梁乃川，乃心乃民，乃寝乃兴，维勇于仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312343_comment'></div>维歙之溪，朝宗于京，江吴荆楚，南东其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312343_comment'></div>淫潦悍湍，两涘千里，有比其舟，坦坦如砥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312343_comment'></div>始谁作之，刘侯炳名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312343_comment'></div>厥既历年，午纵卯横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312343_comment'></div>今侯曰嘻，是不在我，匪用之裕，惟仁之果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312343_comment'></div>虑事属植，乃巡尔功，尔功尔佣，毋失尔农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312343_comment'></div>出斛于庾，百又五十，出缗于府，六万有溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312343_comment'></div>四十其艘，脩六百尺，以今视昔，益三之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312343_comment'></div>治铁为笮，翼其两旁，赋丈倍脩，以时阖张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312343_comment'></div>上春经始，民欢趋之，季月告成，侯来落之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312343_comment'></div>有翩者凫，汎汎涟漪，背负长虹，作鳞之而。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312343_comment'></div>侯曰美哉，既坚既良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312343_comment'></div>民曰允哉，乃康乃庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312343_comment'></div>习坎重险，维其夷矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1312343_comment'></div>过涉灭顶，汔其济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1312343_comment'></div>不川而游，不径而踰，凡人有心，履此正涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1312343_comment'></div>于休我侯，惠我无疆，匪惠伊教，子孙不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1312343_comment'></div>歙山丛丛，其水清写，刻此铭诗，以谂来者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1312343_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　在邵武，作《荷家坞记》<div id='poem_1312342' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312342' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312342?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荷嘉坞记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1253年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312342")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312342_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312342'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312342'>并吾庐而北，有山环焉，版图姓之曰何家坞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312342_comment'></div>自吾之家于斯也，墙其口而圃之而沼之而亭之，盖思所以易其坞名，而芸夫樵子之熟于口，吾易之而彼之不吾易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312342_comment'></div>乃元黓困敦之岁，有莲骈生于其沼，予忻然笑曰，兹其所谓荷嘉坞者与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312342_comment'></div>芸夫樵子之不彼易，则吾易之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312342_comment'></div>于是具著所涂而次序之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312342_comment'></div>凡我同盟，毋惑多岐，一东一西，孰指尔迷，作入山林处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312342_comment'></div>彼痴窟郎，堆钱百屋，我无储胥，一灯夜读，作著图书所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312342_comment'></div>他山有梅，矫矫玉立，不同众芳，春风迟日，作百花头上之亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312342_comment'></div>我秫我田，亦足以酿，西风吹尘，曾莫可向，作归来馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312342_comment'></div>有濯者莲，处污而洁，勿遐尔心，濂溪风月，作君子亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312342_comment'></div>山下出泉，有坎其泚，寒斯冽斯，幽人所履，作寒泓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312342_comment'></div>言抹其刍，田彼荦埆，对眠夕阳，亦勿扣角，作饭牛庵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312342_comment'></div>惟春袅袅，惟夏蹻蹻，惟冬悄悄，惟秋杳杳，作秋崖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312342_comment'></div>耕不一㙻，锄不五亩，耳目口鼻，皆吾之有，作田园居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312342_comment'></div>至是则复于图书所以归吾庐，而山之观止矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312342_comment'></div>方子日一再行，不大风雨不废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312342_comment'></div>顾其老竹穷木非有繁华之奇，草亭茸屋非有榱题之观，而山之豁如，谷之奥如，林岭之翳如，亦有足乐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312342_comment'></div>穿幽逗深，缭绕岚翠，盖穷日之力而后餍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312342_comment'></div>然则声色之蛊其心，孰与禽鸟之适吾情；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312342_comment'></div>轩冕之梏其身，孰与泉石之忘吾形？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312342_comment'></div>当世之名卿材大夫幸得遭时清明，谟格长治，安得而从予游乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312342_comment'></div>乐哉斯丘，山翁野叟之所同而高人胜士之所独也，予其可哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312342_comment'></div>宝祐改元第一日，坞主巨山自记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1312342_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　在邵武，为休宁金文刚之祖父（安节）作《跋金尚书奏稿》<div id='poem_1312317' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312317' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312317?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋金尚书奏藁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1253年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312317")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312317_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312317'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312317'>诚斋跋尾之明年，某实始生，然则于尚书公犹未得为互乡童子也，其所论著，某何敢赘一辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312317_comment'></div>顾无以复命临川史君，则拜手而笔之曰，苏长公有言，问世之治乱必观其人，问其人之贤不肖必以世考之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312317_comment'></div>共惟阜陵之圣，自尧以下无讥焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312317_comment'></div>一时从臣适相会聚，有若我尚书公者四人，而小官之谒吏部铨避而窥屏间者，盖杨诚斋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312317_comment'></div>五人者皆千载人，而同出于一时，呜呼盛哉，此阜陵所以圣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312317_comment'></div>宝祐改元除日，后学方某敬书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1312317_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　在邵武，为嘉禾（嘉兴）曹郸作《在庵记》<div id='poem_1312345' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312345' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312345?labeling=true' target='_blank'>在庵记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1253年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312345")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312345_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312345'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312345'>予归耕穷山，与世不相闻者三年矣，今嘉禾治中曹君郸岁岁焉属记其所谓在庵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312345_comment'></div>君之言曰：「吾家许峰下，故旌阳所尝井臼也，因姓之云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312345_comment'></div>突兀撑空，斗起云海上数千仞，而派其支为小屿，意象闳窈，风气盘互，则不肖孤所以奉吾先君子衣冠之藏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312345_comment'></div>为人子者不敢以其心死其亲，亦不敢以其力俭其亲，则延之而宇之，翼之而榭之，缭之而港之，规之而湖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312345_comment'></div>千嶂所环，岚暝喷薄，迩青远碧，萦幽逗深，吾所不能言者，工所不能画也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312345_comment'></div>吾独能言致思其堂，履濡敬享其室，朝晖暮云其亭，而又著轩焉为斋居，精舍焉为僧馆，最其凡者曰在庵而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312345_comment'></div>吾固也，其惟子之记」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312345_comment'></div>岳惟平川先生以经学为师儒，以论谏为御史，以言议风旨为侍从，天下之名能文章者非其辈则学徒也，顾平生于予文也嗜之尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312345_comment'></div>治中君不彼之诹而予之诿，千数百里走车牛口下而曰，此先志也，其斯之谓在与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312345_comment'></div>一念所存，无在而不在也，立则见其参于前，在舆则见其倚于衡，是谓之在矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312345_comment'></div>正明目以视之而不见，倾耳以听之而不闻，不谓之在乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312345_comment'></div>由前言之则羹墙亦尧，河洛亦禹，凡宸奎宝画、奏篇进卷之藏此山者皆平川也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312345_comment'></div>由后之言，则赤舄非周，蒙倛非孔，其环金植象、形色绘画之留此堂者，谓平川与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312345_comment'></div>「我仪图之，惟仲山甫举之」，平川有焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312345_comment'></div>「惟其有之，是以似之」，治中君勉焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312345_comment'></div>然则所谓在，固在此不在彼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312345_comment'></div>乃若先生之行事，则其状在太常，其传在太史，不书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312345_comment'></div>宝祐改元重阳日，新安方岳书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1312345_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　在邵武，为同邑友谢从之作《顺齐记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　在邵武，《送许允杰序》姑系是年。<span class='inlineComment2'>（许允杰，婺源学者许月卿（字太空，有《山屋集》）之从子。）</span><div id='poem_1312286' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312286' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312286?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送许允杰序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1253年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312286")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312286_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312286'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312286'>往时许太空见予竹西，才洛阳贾生之年耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312286_comment'></div>得其文一通，怪怪奇奇，坐人尽惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312286_comment'></div>亡何以其怪奇者取巍科，怪奇何负于文哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312286_comment'></div>后二十年，太空以书介其从子允杰来见，读其编则亦怪怪奇奇，问其年则亦仅仅陆机入洛之岁，是何许氏之多英妙而怪奇也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312286_comment'></div>予方老退，不得与于斯文，见所谓怪怪奇奇则惊而异耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312286_comment'></div>固尝问太空曰，昌黎谓易奇而法，文奇可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312286_comment'></div>山谷谓奇是文章一病，文奇可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312286_comment'></div>法而不奇，程卫尉之治簿书也，纵无胜亦无败；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312286_comment'></div>奇而不法，李将军之不击刁斗也，不大胜则大败矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312286_comment'></div>其曰文章一病，非与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312286_comment'></div>若归，尽取六经以来至于诸子百氏，以及稗官小说、骚人赋客之所论著，反覆熟之，当自见左氏怪奇于《春秋》，庄骚又怪奇于左氏，子云、相如同工异曲者又怪奇于庄骚，愈降而下之，则文人相高，务为艰涩，难字生语，棘人喉吻，而以不能句读为古，则亦陋矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312286_comment'></div>子其毋文胜而理负，毋言深而意浅，毋论卑而气弱，毋思殆而学罔，则怪怪奇奇将又无负于子矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1312286_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　返里前作《邵武宴交代权部》<div id='poem_1312438' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312438' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312438?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邵武宴交代权郡乐语</a><span class='authorDate'>（1253年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312438")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312438_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312438'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312438'>半刺史行刺史，岂惟风月之分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312438_comment'></div>今将军故将军，共喜星辰之聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312438_comment'></div>碧玉环收霖雨，黄金印领山州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312438_comment'></div>欢奉壶觞，相传衣钵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312438_comment'></div>共惟交代书潜牺极，剑跃龙津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312438_comment'></div>江夏之才无双，幼余有此奇志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312438_comment'></div>颍川之政第一，今何为乎假侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312438_comment'></div>瓜时近在一日间，芝宇飞从九天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312438_comment'></div>小徐王觐，有为民留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312438_comment'></div>谓且握手出肺肝，尚邀阴赐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312438_comment'></div>其将与帝作喉舌，于赫阳光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312438_comment'></div>我知郡式开我龟，乃发尔爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312438_comment'></div>念生平之少可，无今此之佳逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312438_comment'></div>举扇障西风，公毋多问；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312438_comment'></div>持杯劝北斗，夜未渠央。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312438_comment'></div>略驻皓歌，试听舆诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312438_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1312438'>谁作山城三日霖，老天自识两贤心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312438_comment'></div>樵溪留得琴龟住，庐阜飞来笙鹤音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312438_comment'></div>纶绂泥香千里共，裤襦春煖一杯深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312438_comment'></div>薰风辇路重携手，夜对金鸾月满襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312438_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1312438_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宜春

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　在家闲居。起知宁国府，未上，罢。改知袁州（江西宜春）孔凡礼《全宋词补辑》录方岳《江城子》作于是年。<span class='inlineComment2'>（按《洪传》记载知方岳夫人袁州，当在是年七月后。）</span><div id='poem_65062' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_65062' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/65062?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江城子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_65062")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_65062_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_65062'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_65062'>几年诗骨雪槎牙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_65062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_65062'>痼烟霞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_65062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_65062'>老生涯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_65062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_65062'>五十八翁，堪喜亦堪嗟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_65062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_65062'>忽忆香山居士语，还失笑，较争些。<div id='poem_sentence_4_65062_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_65062'>荒寒梅坞月横斜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_65062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_65062'>短篱遮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_65062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_65062'>野人家。<div id='poem_sentence_7_65062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_65062'>枝北枝南，须有两三花。<div id='poem_sentence_8_65062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_65062'>紧闭竹门传语客，那得暇，尽由他。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_65062_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='55597ad0492e426c844ee2338ed5010a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("55597ad0492e426c844ee2338ed5010a");'><span id='55597ad0492e426c844ee2338ed5010a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1259')">1256-1259年</a>，59-62岁</div><div id='55597ad0492e426c844ee2338ed5010a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年8月</a>　在家闲居。起知宁国府，未上，罢。改知袁州（江西宜春）。八月，右相程元凤上疏言人事。岳之被荐知袁州，当从此月始。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　在家闲居。起知宁国府，未上，罢。改知袁州（江西宜春）。方岳孙于是年五月以第一名进士及第，方岳作《石孙受命》<span class='inlineComment2'>（见《小稿诗集》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_64278' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_64278' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/64278?labeling=true' target='_blank'>石孙受命</a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_64278")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_64278_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_64278'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_64278'>圣泽如春雨露宽，弃遗犹不绝衣冠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_64278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_64278'>万钉宝带翁无分，一幅花绫孙有官。<div id='poem_sentence_1_64278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_64278'>得免白丁何啻足，亲曾黄甲不堪看。<div id='poem_sentence_2_64278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_64278'>九经幸自澜翻熟，但守青灯雪屋寒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_64278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_64278'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_64278_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　知袁州。赵与泽知徽州，元月到官。方岳作《与赵寺丞》赞之。<div id='poem_1311967' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1311967' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1311967?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与赵丞书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1311967")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1311967_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1311967'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1311967'>某伏以冬至之日，吾道其亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1311967_comment'></div>恭惟某官涉笔松间，清入雪句，台候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1311967_comment'></div>某望昭亭翠气，叠嶂高寒，其下有人，餐沆瀣而吸朝霞，若将飘飘事外者，盖赵家玉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1311967_comment'></div>祈山底处所乃辱临之，七八年云耕月钓之氓，一旦脱夫须袯襫而去，适相先后旬月耳，士之不相遭如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1311967_comment'></div>刘向汉宗彦，方当校雠天禄，有驾莲叶读玉书之仙，然青藜而下观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1311967_comment'></div>虽某凡骨，或者得于此时见之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1311967_comment'></div>受塍一廛，见大夫洒墨先之，某知罪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1311967_comment'></div>绨袭藏去，惭感渠央。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1311967_comment'></div>葭莩浮春，玉辑均祉，某疏且贱者不敢僭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1311967_comment'></div>此有凡役，愿与闻之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1311967_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　知袁州。祁门宰费翊上年卒于任，是年元月葬，应其从弟平江府司法参军翿之请，方岳作《知县奉议费公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1312378' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312378' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312378?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知县奉议费公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝祐四年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26438, "南宋", "方岳", "poem_title_1312378")'>方岳</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312378_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312378'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312378'>祈门蕞尔邑，然士大夫初脱选，以名次须入者相传为佳缺，谓县无逋，郡易办，民亦无县挠，易治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312378_comment'></div>不知何以自十数年来，筑底不复可错乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312378_comment'></div>巽愞者不竞，健决者不恤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312378_comment'></div>乃岁癸丑，令以忧去，未知新令谁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312378_comment'></div>丞摄其事，民重足立且期月，而毗陵费公实来，盖恂恂似不能言而人知其慈，偲偲然不敢名一钱而人知其廉，吾民其庶几乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312378_comment'></div>居亡何，丞自上府白事，不知道何等语，归则檄与令同督赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312378_comment'></div>于是钱不府，帛不库，诞寘之崔斯立壁记下，自出入之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312378_comment'></div>已乃遣文书诣令，令顾涉笔惟谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312378_comment'></div>令有所书注或不可丞意，丞辄涂窜之略尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312378_comment'></div>予尝为公不平，公独无几微见颜面，退然后惭予浅之为丈夫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312378_comment'></div>会绣衣使者行部，廉治丞狱，公始得为县，而县甚不可为矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312378_comment'></div>官有欠籍，民无逋租，悍吏持急符来，隳突堂奥，刻木者鸟兽散，令噤不敢一出声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312378_comment'></div>公于其间，岂能无邑邑，而竟以殁，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312378_comment'></div>盖宝祐三年夏六月庚寅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312378_comment'></div>公讳羾，字叔羽，无锡人，自唐昭宗阙律郎球者家文笔峰下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312378_comment'></div>至肃以上舍郎与简斋陈公齐名，建炎初两人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312378_comment'></div>起，终左朝散郎，赠通奉大夫，娶陈氏，为曾大父；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312378_comment'></div>锴，登绍兴十一年进士第，提举福建市舶，赠开府仪同三司，娶蒋氏、和国夫人，是为大父；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312378_comment'></div>培，中大夫、秘阁修撰，赠少傅，娶郤氏，吉国夫人，陈氏，卫国夫人，是为父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312378_comment'></div>公其第三子也，阶自通仕郎至奉议郎，历监嘉兴府都税务、抚州金陵县丞、监行在省仓上界、监太平惠民北局、知徽州祈门县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312378_comment'></div>始公改秩，加职司一员为尤伟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312378_comment'></div>丞金溪时，宜黄群盗辈捕之得，则十六人者杀越人于货，辞具服等死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312378_comment'></div>部使者移公谳之，特其中一人黄姓者真盗耳，馀尽诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1312378_comment'></div>一平反活十五人，岂非贤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1312378_comment'></div>前所谓丞得罪时，常情不下石亦击节矣，公方为携其印纸历尾使者车解和之，得还其历，谓绛侯、东阳侯长者非与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1312378_comment'></div>娶陈氏，封孺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1312378_comment'></div>三子：逵、逊、逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1312378_comment'></div>四女，适迪功郎、监浙西安抚司回易库钱昌言，其适承务郎钱谟者未行，馀幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1312378_comment'></div>以宝祐四年正月二十七日，葬于本邑长腰山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1312378_comment'></div>从弟从政郎、新平江府司法参军翿来请铭，辞不可则诺，意某氓也其言信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1312378_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1312378'>维鹊有巢，维鸠居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1312378_comment'></div>谁寔尹我，丞则躨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1312378_comment'></div>尔毋我躨，我尹我慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1312378_comment'></div>慈如之何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1312378_comment'></div>既疮且痍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1312378_comment'></div>问之在民，民无宿逋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1312378_comment'></div>问之在官，官有急符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1312378_comment'></div>尔狱痡矣，我尹殂矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1312378_comment'></div>奚而殂而，喟其吁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1312378_comment'></div>有暴如虎，有慈如母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1312378_comment'></div>虎犹我怒，母不我怙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1312378_comment'></div>谓天孔明，公独我怙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1312378_comment'></div>作铭者氓，可信千古。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1312378_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年</a>　在袁州，后除尚书左郎官。程元凤罢想，出判福州，丁大全挟嫌报复。李曾伯原与方岳有交，今任广南制置大使兼知静江府，故有“辟充参谋”之举。方岳未就，改除尚书左郎官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年</a>　在袁州，后除尚书左郎官。方岳作《春日乘舆》十五首。其五结句有云：“寒期雪屋青灯夜，六十尤痴始是痴”似有悔其出山之意。十五首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《小稿诗集》卷一九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年</a>　改除尚书左郎官后，定大全嗾九江制置副使袁玠弹劾罢之。<br /></div>
-----end
